"""
SOC Access Management Tool (CLI First, GUI Optional)
----------------------------------------------------
Provides a simple interface for SOC access management:
- Check User Access
- Grant User Access
- Remove User Access
- Clear RT Ticket Queue

🛠️ Designed for **command-line operation** with an optional GUI.
✅ Aligned with Matt's goal: **simplicity, maintainability, and clarity**.
"""

import sys
import os
import subprocess
import threading
import logging

# GUI Dependencies (Optional)
try:
    import tkinter as tk
    from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext
except ImportError:
    print("Tkinter is not installed. Run scripts via CLI instead.")
    sys.exit()

# Set up base directories
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get the script's directory
LOGS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Logs")
UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils")  # Locate utilities directory

# Ensure Logs directory exists
if not os.path.exists(LOGS_DIR):
    os.makedirs(LOGS_DIR)

# Add Utils directory to Python path for importing rt_api.py
sys.path.insert(0, UTILS_DIR)

# Import RT API functionality
try:
    from rt_api import add_comment
except ModuleNotFoundError as e:
    print(f"❌ Error: Could not import rt_api. Make sure Utils/ is in the correct location.\n{e}")
    sys.exit(1)

# Set up logging
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOGS_DIR, "soctool.log")
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, level=logging.INFO, format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s")

# Define paths to access management scripts
CHECK_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "checkaccess.py")
GRANT_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "grantaccess.py")
REMOVE_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "separation.py")
CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "close_cleared_rts.py")

# CLI Mode: Provide usage instructions
if len(sys.argv) > 1:
    print("\nSOC Access Management Tool (CLI First, GUI Optional)")
    print("====================================================")
    print("Usage:")
    print("  python soctool.py   # Starts the GUI (optional)")
    print("  python checkaccess.py <ldap_user> <ldap_pass> <target_user> --rt_ticket <ticket_number>")
    print("  python grantaccess.py <ldap_user> <ldap_pass> <target_user> --mock --rt_ticket <ticket_number>")
    print("  python separation.py <ldap_user> <ldap_pass> <target_user> --mock --rt_ticket <ticket_number>")
    print("  python close_cleared_rts.py   # Clears resolved RT tickets")
    sys.exit()  # Exit CLI mode

def execute_script(script_path, args, log_area):
    """Executes an external script and updates log output in the GUI."""
    def run(args_copy):  # ✅ Explicitly pass args_copy to avoid UnboundLocalError
        try:
            if args_copy is None:
                args_copy = []

            args_copy = [arg for arg in args_copy if arg]  # ✅ Remove None/empty args

            # ✅ Use Popen with real-time output streaming
            process = subprocess.Popen(
                ["python", script_path] + args_copy,
                stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
                stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
                text=True,
                encoding="utf-8"
            )

            # ✅ Read stdout and stderr line by line to ensure real-time output in GUI
            for line in iter(process.stdout.readline, ""):
                log_area.insert(tk.END, line)
                log_area.see(tk.END)

            for line in iter(process.stderr.readline, ""):
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"⚠️ {line}")
                log_area.see(tk.END)

            process.stdout.close()
            process.stderr.close()
            process.wait()

            logging.info(f"Executed {script_path} with args: {args_copy}")

        except Exception as e:
            log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {str(e)}\n")
            logging.error(f"Error executing {script_path}: {str(e)}")

    # ✅ Explicitly pass args to avoid UnboundLocalError
    threading.Thread(target=run, args=(args,), daemon=True).start()

def check_access(username, ldap_user, ldap_pass, rt_ticket=None):
    """
    Checks a user's access across multiple SOC systems.

    Args:
        username (str): The LDAP username to check.
        ldap_user (str): The SOC user's LDAP username.
        ldap_pass (str): The SOC user's LDAP password.
        rt_ticket (str, optional): RT ticket number for logging results.

    Returns:
        str: Formatted output containing all access results.
    """

    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    logging.info(f"===== START: {timestamp} - Checking Access for {username} =====")

    results = [f"🔹 Access check for {username} at {timestamp}\n"]  # Store access check results

    # ✅ Loop through all scripts in the Systems directory
    if os.path.exists(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        for script in os.listdir(SYSTEMS_DIR):
            if script.endswith(".py"):  # Run all scripts (including adtrack.py)
                system_name = script.replace(".py", "").capitalize()
                script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)

                print(f"🔍 Running system check: {script_path}")  # Debugging

                try:
                    process = subprocess.Popen(
                        ["python", script_path, username],
                        stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
                        stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
                        text=True,
                        encoding="utf-8"
                    )

                    stdout_output, stderr_output = process.communicate()

                    if stdout_output:
                        results.append(f"✅ {system_name}: {stdout_output.strip()}")
                        logging.info(f"{system_name} - {stdout_output.strip()}")

                    if stderr_output:
                        results.append(f"⚠️ {system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")
                        logging.error(f"{system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")

                except Exception as e:
                    results.append(f"❌ {system_name}: Error running script - {e}")
                    logging.error(f"Error running {system_name} script: {e}")

    else:
        error_msg = "❌ Error: 'Systems/' directory not found."
        results.append(error_msg)
        logging.error(error_msg)

    # ✅ Summarize results
    summary = "\n".join(results)

    # ✅ Log results to an RT ticket if provided
    if rt_ticket:
        add_comment(rt_ticket, summary)

    logging.info(f"===== END: {timestamp} - Check Completed for {username} =====\n")

    # ✅ Return summary so it appears in GUI
    print(summary)  # ✅ Ensures soctool.py captures this output
    return summary  # ✅ Ensure soctool.py correctly receives results



if __name__ == "__main__":
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Check user access across SOC systems.")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_user", help="Your LDAP username")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_pass", help="Your LDAP password")
    parser.add_argument("username", help="LDAP username of the user to check")
    parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT Ticket number for documentation", nargs="?", default=None)

    args = parser.parse_args()

    rt_ticket = args.rt_ticket if args.rt_ticket else None

    # ✅ Run check_access and print results to CLI
    output = check_access(args.username, args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass, rt_ticket)
    print(output)  # ✅ Ensure output is captured by soctool.py






import logging
import psycopg2
import os
import subprocess

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ Dashlane CLI Path
DASHLANE_CLI_PATH = "C:\\Program Files\\DashlaneCLI\\dashlane.exe"

def get_dashlane_note(note_title):
    """Retrieve credentials stored in Dashlane Secure Note."""
    try:
        result = subprocess.run(
            [DASHLANE_CLI_PATH, "note", note_title],
            capture_output=True,
            text=True,
            check=True
        )

        lines = result.stdout.strip().split("\n")  # Split into lines
        if len(lines) < 2:
            logging.error("❌ Dashlane note does not contain expected credentials format!")
            return None, None

        return lines[0].strip(), lines[1].strip()  # Username, Password

    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to retrieve Dashlane note '{note_title}': {e}")
        return None, None

# ✅ Retrieve database credentials from Dashlane Secure Note
ADTRACK_DB_USER, ADTRACK_DB_PASS = get_dashlane_note("SOC - AdTrack Credentials")

DB_CONFIG = {
    "dbname": "adtrack_ro",
    "host": "vspool.som1.marchex.com",
    "port": 5432,
    "user": ADTRACK_DB_USER,
    "password": ADTRACK_DB_PASS
}

def get_db_connection():
    """Establish a database connection to AdTrack."""
    if not DB_CONFIG["user"] or not DB_CONFIG["password"]:
        logging.error("❌ Database credentials not found in Dashlane! Ensure Dashlane CLI is logged in.")
        return None

    try:
        return psycopg2.connect(**DB_CONFIG)
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Database connection failed: {e}")
        return None

def check_adtrack_access(user, vendor_email=None):
    """Check if a user has AdTrack UI access."""
    search_param = vendor_email or f"{user}@marchex.com"

    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        return None

    query = "SELECT email FROM at_user WHERE email ILIKE %s AND status != 'disabled'"
    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute(query, (search_param,))
            result = cur.fetchall()

        conn.close()
        return [row[0] for row in result] if result else None

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Database query failed: {e}")
        return None

def main():
    """Run the script for checking AdTrack UI access."""
    sep_list = input("Enter LDAP user(s) to check (comma-separated): ").split(",")
    is_vendor = input("Is this user a vendor? (Yes/No): ").strip().lower()
    vendor_email = input("Enter vendor email address: ") if is_vendor == "yes" else None

    for user in sep_list:
        user = user.strip()
        access = check_adtrack_access(user, vendor_email)

        if access:
            logging.info(f"✅ {user} has AdTrack UI access: {access}")
        else:
            logging.info(f"❌ {user} does NOT have AdTrack UI access.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

"""
SOC Access Management Tool (CLI First, GUI Optional)
----------------------------------------------------
Provides a simple interface for SOC access management:
- Check User Access
- Grant User Access
- Remove User Access
- Clear RT Ticket Queue

🛠️ Designed for **command-line operation** with an optional GUI.
✅ Aligned with Matt's goal: **simplicity, maintainability, and clarity**.
"""

import sys
import os
import subprocess
import threading
import logging

# GUI Dependencies (Optional)
try:
    import tkinter as tk
    from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext
except ImportError:
    print("Tkinter is not installed. Run scripts via CLI instead.")
    sys.exit()

# Set up base directories
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get the script's directory
LOGS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Logs")
UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils")  # Locate utilities directory

# Ensure Logs directory exists
if not os.path.exists(LOGS_DIR):
    os.makedirs(LOGS_DIR)

# Add Utils directory to Python path for importing rt_api.py
sys.path.insert(0, UTILS_DIR)

# Import RT API functionality
try:
    from rt_api import add_comment
except ModuleNotFoundError as e:
    print(f"❌ Error: Could not import rt_api. Make sure Utils/ is in the correct location.\n{e}")
    sys.exit(1)

# Set up logging
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOGS_DIR, "soctool.log")
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, level=logging.INFO, format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s")

# Define paths to access management scripts
CHECK_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "checkaccess.py")
GRANT_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "grantaccess.py")
REMOVE_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "separation.py")
CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "close_cleared_rts.py")

# CLI Mode: Provide usage instructions
if len(sys.argv) > 1:
    print("\nSOC Access Management Tool (CLI First, GUI Optional)")
    print("====================================================")
    print("Usage:")
    print("  python soctool.py   # Starts the GUI (optional)")
    print("  python checkaccess.py <ldap_user> <ldap_pass> <target_user> --rt_ticket <ticket_number>")
    print("  python grantaccess.py <ldap_user> <ldap_pass> <target_user> --mock --rt_ticket <ticket_number>")
    print("  python separation.py <ldap_user> <ldap_pass> <target_user> --mock --rt_ticket <ticket_number>")
    print("  python close_cleared_rts.py   # Clears resolved RT tickets")
    sys.exit()  # Exit CLI mode

def execute_script(script_path, args, log_area):
    """Executes an external script and updates log output in the GUI."""
    def run(args_copy):  
        try:
            process = subprocess.Popen(
                ["python", script_path] + args_copy,
                stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
                stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
                text=True,
                encoding="utf-8",
                bufsize=1  # ✅ Prevents output buffering
            )

            # ✅ Capture stdout and stderr in real-time
            while True:
                line = process.stdout.readline()
                if not line:
                    break
                log_area.insert(tk.END, line)
                log_area.see(tk.END)

            while True:
                line = process.stderr.readline()
                if not line:
                    break
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"⚠️ {line}")
                log_area.see(tk.END)

            process.stdout.close()
            process.stderr.close()
            process.wait()

        except Exception as e:
            log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {str(e)}\n")
            logging.error(f"Error executing {script_path}: {str(e)}")

    threading.Thread(target=run, args=(args,), daemon=True).start()


    
def open_access_window(action, script_path, show_mock_mode=True):
    """
    Opens a GUI window for user access management.

    Args:
        action (str): "Check", "Grant", or "Remove" (determines window title and action).
        script_path (str): Path to the corresponding script.
        show_mock_mode (bool): Whether to show the mock mode checkbox (only for Grant and Remove).
    """

    action_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    action_window.title(f"SOC - {action} Access")
    action_window.geometry("500x525")

    tk.Label(action_window, text=f"{action} User Access", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    # LDAP Credentials
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:").pack()
    ldap_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP password:").pack()
    ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40, show="*")  # Hide password input
    ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Target User
    tk.Label(action_window, text=f"Enter LDAP username to {action.lower()} access for:").pack()
    target_user_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    target_user_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # RT Ticket Number (Optional)
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter RT Ticket Number (Optional):").pack()
    rt_ticket_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    rt_ticket_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Mock Mode Toggle (only shown for Grant and Remove)
    mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=True)
    if show_mock_mode:
        tk.Checkbutton(action_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode).pack()

    # Log Display
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Logs:").pack()
    log_area = tk.Text(action_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    def execute_action(event=None):
        ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()
        ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()
        target_user = target_user_entry.get().strip()
        rt_ticket = rt_ticket_entry.get().strip() if rt_ticket_entry.get().strip() else None
        mock_flag = "--mock" if show_mock_mode and mock_mode.get() else ""

        if not ldap_user or not ldap_pass or not target_user:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "All fields are required except RT Ticket.")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Running {action} script for {target_user}...\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        # ✅ Properly format arguments
        args = [ldap_user, ldap_pass, target_user]
        if rt_ticket:
            args.extend(["--rt_ticket", rt_ticket])  # ✅ Add optional argument properly
        if mock_flag:
            args.append(mock_flag)

        execute_script(script_path, args, log_area)
        
    tk.Button(action_window, text="Execute", command=execute_action, font=("Arial", 12), width=20).pack(pady=10)
    action_window.bind("<Return>", execute_action)

def open_clear_rt_window():
    """
    Opens a GUI window to display RT queue clearing process in real-time.
    """

    rt_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    rt_window.title("Clearing RT Queue")
    rt_window.geometry("600x400")

    tk.Label(rt_window, text="Processing RT Queue...", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    # Log Display
    log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(rt_window, width=70, height=15)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    execute_script(CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT, [], log_area)

# GUI Window Setup
root = tk.Tk()
root.title("SOC Access Management")
root.geometry("400x350")
root.resizable(False, False)

# Header
tk.Label(root, text="SOC Access Management", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=20)

# Buttons to trigger scripts
tk.Button(root, text="Check User Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("Check", CHECK_ACCESS_SCRIPT, show_mock_mode=False), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Grant User Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("Grant", GRANT_ACCESS_SCRIPT, show_mock_mode=True), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Remove User Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("Remove", REMOVE_ACCESS_SCRIPT, show_mock_mode=True), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Clear RT Queue", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_clear_rt_window(), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

# Start GUI
root.mainloop()




"""
SOC Access Check Script (CLI Only)
-----------------------------------------
Checks a user's access across multiple SOC systems.

🛠️ Features:
- Runs system-specific access checks via external scripts.
- Logs results in Logs/SOC_Access_Log.txt.
- Automatically updates an RT ticket (if provided).
✅ **Designed for CLI operation only.** GUI is handled separately in soctool.py.
"""

import argparse
import logging
import os
import subprocess
import sys
from datetime import datetime

# ✅ Ensure UTF-8 encoding (prevents UnicodeEncodeError)
sys.stdout.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")
sys.stderr.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")
sys.stdin.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")

# ✅ Set up base directories
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get current script location
UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils")  # Locate Utils folder
SYSTEMS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems")  # Locate Systems folder
LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Logs")  # Correct path to Logs/

# ✅ Ensure directories exist
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)  # Create Logs/ directory if missing
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.abspath(UTILS_DIR))  # Add Utils to Python path

# ✅ Attempt to import rt_api.py
try:
    from rt_api import add_comment  # Import RT API functionality
except ModuleNotFoundError as e:
    print(f"❌ Error: Could not import rt_api. Ensure 'Utils/' is inside 'soctool/' and properly structured.\n{e}")
    sys.exit(1)

# ✅ Set up logging
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "SOC_Access_Log.txt")
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s', level=logging.INFO)


def check_access(username, ldap_user, ldap_pass, rt_ticket=None):
    """
    Checks a user's access across multiple SOC systems.

    Args:
        username (str): The LDAP username to check.
        ldap_user (str): The SOC user's LDAP username.
        ldap_pass (str): The SOC user's LDAP password.
        rt_ticket (str, optional): RT ticket number for logging results.

    Returns:
        str: Formatted output containing all access results.
    """

    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    logging.info(f"===== START: {timestamp} - Checking Access for {username} =====")

    results = [f"🔹 Access check for {username} at {timestamp}\n"]  # Store access check results
    script_count = 0  # Track how many scripts run

    if not os.path.exists(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        error_msg = "❌ Error: 'Systems/' directory not found."
        results.append(error_msg)
        logging.error(error_msg)
        print("\n".join(results))  # ✅ Print output so GUI can capture it
        sys.stdout.flush()  # ✅ Ensure output reaches soctool.py
        return "\n".join(results)

    # ✅ Run all scripts in Systems directory
    for script in os.listdir(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        if script.endswith(".py"):  
            system_name = script.replace(".py", "").capitalize()
            script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)

            try:
                process = subprocess.Popen(
                    ["python", script_path, username],
                    stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
                    stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
                    text=True,
                    encoding="utf-8",
                    bufsize=1  # ✅ Ensure real-time streaming of output
                )

                stdout_output, stderr_output = process.communicate()

                if stdout_output.strip():
                    results.append(f"✅ {system_name}: {stdout_output.strip()}")
                    logging.info(f"{system_name} - {stdout_output.strip()}")

                if stderr_output.strip():
                    results.append(f"⚠️ {system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")
                    logging.error(f"{system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")

            except Exception as e:
                results.append(f"❌ {system_name}: Error running script - {e}")
                logging.error(f"Error running {system_name} script: {e}")

    summary = "\n".join(results)

    # ✅ Log results to an RT ticket if provided
    if rt_ticket:
        add_comment(rt_ticket, summary)

    logging.info(f"===== END: {timestamp} - Check Completed for {username} =====\n")

    print(summary)  # ✅ Ensure this output reaches soctool.py
    sys.stdout.flush()  # ✅ Force output to be captured in GUI
    return summary  # ✅ Ensure soctool.py correctly receives results



if __name__ == "__main__":
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Check user access across SOC systems.")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_user", help="Your LDAP username")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_pass", help="Your LDAP password")
    parser.add_argument("username", help="LDAP username of the user to check")
    parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT Ticket number for documentation", nargs="?", default=None)

    args = parser.parse_args()
    check_access(args.username, args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass, args.rt_ticket)
    rt_ticket = args.rt_ticket if args.rt_ticket else None

    # ✅ Run check_access and print results to CLI
    output = check_access(args.username, args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass, rt_ticket)
    print(output)  # ✅ Ensure output is captured by soctool.py

logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, level=logging.INFO, format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s")

if len(sys.argv) > 1:
    print("\nSOC Access Management Tool (CLI First, GUI Optional)")
    print("====================================================")
    print("Usage:")
    print("  python soctool.py   # Starts the GUI (optional)")
    print("  python checkaccess.py <ldap_user> <ldap_pass> <target_user> --rt_ticket <ticket_number>")
    print("  python grantaccess.py <ldap_user> <ldap_pass> <target_user> --mock --rt_ticket <ticket_number>")
    print("  python separation.py <ldap_user> <ldap_pass> <target_user> --mock --rt_ticket <ticket_number>")
    print("  python close_cleared_rts.py   # Clears resolved RT tickets")
    sys.exit()  # Exit CLI mode

def execute_script(script_path, args, log_area):
    """Executes an external script and updates log output in the GUI."""
    
    def run():
        try:
            # ✅ Ensure output is streamed properly
            process = subprocess.Popen(
                ["python", script_path] + args,
                stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
                stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
                text=True,
                encoding="utf-8",
                bufsize=1  # Prevents output buffering
            )

            # ✅ Capture stdout in real-time and ensure single execution
            for line in iter(process.stdout.readline, ""):
                log_area.insert(tk.END, line)  # Only append new logs
                log_area.see(tk.END)

            for line in iter(process.stderr.readline, ""):
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"⚠️ {line}")
                log_area.see(tk.END)

            process.stdout.close()
            process.stderr.close()
            process.wait()

        except Exception as e:
            log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {str(e)}\n")
            logging.error(f"Error executing {script_path}: {str(e)}")

    # ✅ Start a single thread to prevent multiple executions
    thread = threading.Thread(target=run, daemon=True)
    thread.start()


    
def open_access_window(action, script_path, show_mock_mode=True):
    """
    Opens a GUI window for user access management.

    Args:
        action (str): "Check", "Grant", or "Remove" (determines window title and action).
        script_path (str): Path to the corresponding script.
        show_mock_mode (bool): Whether to show the mock mode checkbox (only for Grant and Remove).
    """

    action_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    action_window.title(f"SOC - {action} Access")
    action_window.geometry("500x525")

    tk.Label(action_window, text=f"{action} User Access", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    # LDAP Credentials
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:").pack()
    ldap_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP password:").pack()
    ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40, show="*")  # Hide password input
    ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Target User
    tk.Label(action_window, text=f"Enter LDAP username to {action.lower()} access for:").pack()
    target_user_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    target_user_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # RT Ticket Number (Optional)
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter RT Ticket Number (Optional):").pack()
    rt_ticket_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    rt_ticket_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Mock Mode Toggle (only shown for Grant and Remove)
    mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=True)
    if show_mock_mode:
        tk.Checkbutton(action_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode).pack()

    # Log Display
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Logs:").pack()
    log_area = tk.Text(action_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    def execute_action(event=None):
        ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()
        ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()
        target_user = target_user_entry.get().strip()
        rt_ticket = rt_ticket_entry.get().strip() if rt_ticket_entry.get().strip() else None
        mock_flag = "--mock" if show_mock_mode and mock_mode.get() else ""

        if not ldap_user or not ldap_pass or not target_user:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "All fields are required except RT Ticket.")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Running {action} script for {target_user}...\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        # ✅ Properly format arguments
        args = [ldap_user, ldap_pass, target_user]
        if rt_ticket:
            args.extend(["--rt_ticket", rt_ticket])  # ✅ Add optional argument properly
        if mock_flag:
            args.append(mock_flag)

        execute_script(script_path, args, log_area)
        
    tk.Button(action_window, text="Execute", command=execute_action, font=("Arial", 12), width=20).pack(pady=10)
    action_window.bind("<Return>", execute_action)

def open_clear_rt_window():
    """
    Opens a GUI window to display RT queue clearing process in real-time.
    """

    rt_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    rt_window.title("Clearing RT Queue")
    rt_window.geometry("600x400")

    tk.Label(rt_window, text="Processing RT Queue...", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    # Log Display
    log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(rt_window, width=70, height=15)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    execute_script(CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT, [], log_area)

# GUI Window Setup
root = tk.Tk()
root.title("SOC Access Management")
root.geometry("400x350")
root.resizable(False, False)

# Header
tk.Label(root, text="SOC Access Management", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=20)

# Buttons to trigger scripts
tk.Button(root, text="Check User Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("Check", CHECK_ACCESS_SCRIPT, show_mock_mode=False), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Grant User Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("Grant", GRANT_ACCESS_SCRIPT, show_mock_mode=True), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Remove User Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("Remove", REMOVE_ACCESS_SCRIPT, show_mock_mode=True), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Clear RT Queue", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_clear_rt_window(), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

# Start GUI
root.mainloop()




"""
SOC Access Check Script (CLI Only)
-----------------------------------------
Checks a user's access across multiple SOC systems.

🛠️ Features:
- Runs system-specific access checks via external scripts.
- Logs results in Logs/SOC_Access_Log.txt.
- Automatically updates an RT ticket (if provided).
✅ **Designed for CLI operation only.** GUI is handled separately in soctool.py.
"""

import argparse
import logging
import os
import subprocess
import sys
from datetime import datetime

# ✅ Ensure UTF-8 encoding (prevents UnicodeEncodeError)
sys.stdout.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")
sys.stderr.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")
sys.stdin.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")

# ✅ Set up base directories
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get current script location
UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils")  # Locate Utils folder
SYSTEMS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems")  # Locate Systems folder
LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Logs")  # Correct path to Logs/

# ✅ Ensure directories exist
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)  # Create Logs/ directory if missing
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.abspath(UTILS_DIR))  # Add Utils to Python path

# ✅ Attempt to import rt_api.py
try:
    from rt_api import add_comment  # Import RT API functionality
except ModuleNotFoundError as e:
    print(f"❌ Error: Could not import rt_api. Ensure 'Utils/' is inside 'soctool/' and properly structured.\n{e}")
    sys.exit(1)

# ✅ Set up logging
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "SOC_Access_Log.txt")
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s', level=logging.INFO)


def check_access(username, ldap_user, ldap_pass, rt_ticket=None):
    """
    Runs system-specific access checks and ensures output is correctly returned.
    """

    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    results = [f"🔹 Access check for {username} at {timestamp}"]

    if not os.path.exists(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        error_msg = "❌ Error: 'Systems/' directory not found."
        results.append(error_msg)
        logging.error(error_msg)
        print("\n".join(results))
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return "\n".join(results)

    # ✅ Run each system check script once
    for script in os.listdir(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        if script.endswith(".py"):  
            system_name = script.replace(".py", "").capitalize()
            script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)

            try:
                process = subprocess.Popen(
                    ["python", script_path, username],
                    stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
                    stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
                    text=True,
                    encoding="utf-8",
                    bufsize=1
                )

                stdout_output, stderr_output = process.communicate()

                if stdout_output.strip():
                    results.append(f"✅ {system_name}: {stdout_output.strip()}")
                    logging.info(f"{system_name} - {stdout_output.strip()}")

                if stderr_output.strip():
                    results.append(f"⚠️ {system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")
                    logging.error(f"{system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")

            except Exception as e:
                results.append(f"❌ {system_name}: Error running script - {e}")
                logging.error(f"Error running {system_name} script: {e}")

    summary = "\n".join(results)
    
    # ✅ Print once so soctool.py correctly captures it
    print(summary)
    sys.stdout.flush()
    
    return summary




if __name__ == "__main__":
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Check user access across SOC systems.")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_user", help="Your LDAP username")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_pass", help="Your LDAP password")
    parser.add_argument("username", help="LDAP username of the user to check")
    parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT Ticket number for documentation", nargs="?", default=None)

    args = parser.parse_args()
    check_access(args.username, args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass, args.rt_ticket)
    rt_ticket = args.rt_ticket if args.rt_ticket else None

    # ✅ Run check_access and print results to CLI
    output = check_access(args.username, args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass, rt_ticket)
    print(output)  # ✅ Ensure output is captured by soctool.py






import logging
import psycopg2
import os
import subprocess

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ Dashlane CLI Path
DASHLANE_CLI_PATH = "C:\\Program Files\\DashlaneCLI\\dashlane.exe"

def get_dashlane_note(note_title):
    """Retrieve credentials stored in Dashlane Secure Note."""
    try:
        result = subprocess.run(
            [DASHLANE_CLI_PATH, "note", note_title],
            capture_output=True,
            text=True,
            check=True
        )

        lines = result.stdout.strip().split("\n")  # Split into lines
        if len(lines) < 2:
            logging.error("❌ Dashlane note does not contain expected credentials format!")
            return None, None

        return lines[0].strip(), lines[1].strip()  # Username, Password

    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to retrieve Dashlane note '{note_title}': {e}")
        return None, None

# ✅ Retrieve database credentials from Dashlane Secure Note
ADTRACK_DB_USER, ADTRACK_DB_PASS = get_dashlane_note("SOC - AdTrack Credentials")

DB_CONFIG = {
    "dbname": "adtrack_ro",
    "host": "vspool.som1.marchex.com",
    "port": 5432,
    "user": ADTRACK_DB_USER,
    "password": ADTRACK_DB_PASS
}

def get_db_connection():
    """Establish a database connection to AdTrack."""
    if not DB_CONFIG["user"] or not DB_CONFIG["password"]:
        logging.error("❌ Database credentials not found in Dashlane! Ensure Dashlane CLI is logged in.")
        return None

    try:
        return psycopg2.connect(**DB_CONFIG)
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Database connection failed: {e}")
        return None

def check_adtrack_access(user, vendor_email=None):
    """Check if a user has AdTrack UI access."""
    search_param = vendor_email or f"{user}@marchex.com"

    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        return None

    query = "SELECT email FROM at_user WHERE email ILIKE %s AND status != 'disabled'"
    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute(query, (search_param,))
            result = cur.fetchall()

        conn.close()
        return [row[0] for row in result] if result else None

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Database query failed: {e}")
        return None

def main():
    """Check AdTrack UI access and return results correctly."""
    
    user = input("Enter LDAP user to check: ").strip()
    is_vendor = input("Is this user a vendor? (Yes/No): ").strip().lower()
    vendor_email = input("Enter vendor email address: ") if is_vendor == "yes" else None

    access = check_adtrack_access(user, vendor_email)

    if access:
        result = f"✅ {user} has AdTrack UI access: {access}"
        logging.info(result)
    else:
        result = f"❌ {user} does NOT have AdTrack UI access."
        logging.info(result)

    # ✅ Ensure output prints correctly so it reaches checkaccess.py
    print(result)
    sys.stdout.flush()  # Ensures output is captured correctly

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

"""
SOC Access Management Tool (CLI First, GUI Optional)
----------------------------------------------------
Provides a simple interface for SOC access management:
- Check User Access
- Grant User Access
- Remove User Access
- Clear RT Ticket Queue

🛠️ Designed for **command-line operation** with an optional GUI.
✅ Aligned with Matt's goal: **simplicity, maintainability, and clarity**.
"""

import sys
import os
import subprocess
import threading
import logging

# GUI Dependencies (Optional)
try:
    import tkinter as tk
    from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext
except ImportError:
    print("Tkinter is not installed. Run scripts via CLI instead.")
    sys.exit()

# Set up base directories
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get the script's directory
LOGS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Logs")
UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils")  # Locate utilities directory

# Ensure Logs directory exists
if not os.path.exists(LOGS_DIR):
    os.makedirs(LOGS_DIR)

# Add Utils directory to Python path for importing rt_api.py
sys.path.insert(0, UTILS_DIR)

# Import RT API functionality
try:
    from rt_api import add_comment
except ModuleNotFoundError as e:
    print(f"❌ Error: Could not import rt_api. Make sure Utils/ is in the correct location.\n{e}")
    sys.exit(1)

# Set up logging
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOGS_DIR, "soctool.log")
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, level=logging.INFO, format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s")

# Define paths to access management scripts
CHECK_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "checkaccess.py")
GRANT_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "grantaccess.py")
REMOVE_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "separation.py")
CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "close_cleared_rts.py")

# CLI Mode: Provide usage instructions
if len(sys.argv) > 1:
    print("\nSOC Access Management Tool (CLI First, GUI Optional)")
    print("====================================================")
    print("Usage:")
    print("  python soctool.py   # Starts the GUI (optional)")
    print("  python checkaccess.py <ldap_user> <ldap_pass> <target_user> --rt_ticket <ticket_number>")
    print("  python grantaccess.py <ldap_user> <ldap_pass> <target_user> --mock --rt_ticket <ticket_number>")
    print("  python separation.py <ldap_user> <ldap_pass> <target_user> --mock --rt_ticket <ticket_number>")
    print("  python close_cleared_rts.py   # Clears resolved RT tickets")
    sys.exit()  # Exit CLI mode

def execute_script(script_path, args, log_area):
    """Executes an external script **only once** and updates log output in the GUI."""
    
    def run():
        try:
            # ✅ Ensure output is streamed properly
            process = subprocess.Popen(
                ["python", script_path] + args,
                stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
                stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
                text=True,
                encoding="utf-8",
                bufsize=1  # Prevents output buffering
            )

            log_seen = set()  # ✅ Avoid duplicate log entries

            # ✅ Capture stdout in real-time and ensure single execution
            for line in iter(process.stdout.readline, ""):
                line = line.strip()
                if line and line not in log_seen:
                    log_seen.add(line)
                    log_area.insert(tk.END, line + "\n")  # Only append new logs
                    log_area.see(tk.END)

            for line in iter(process.stderr.readline, ""):
                line = line.strip()
                if line and line not in log_seen:
                    log_seen.add(line)
                    log_area.insert(tk.END, f"⚠️ {line}\n")
                    log_area.see(tk.END)

            process.stdout.close()
            process.stderr.close()
            process.wait()

        except Exception as e:
            log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {str(e)}\n")
            logging.error(f"Error executing {script_path}: {str(e)}")

    # ✅ Start a single thread **only if it's not already running**
    if not threading.active_count() > 1:
        thread = threading.Thread(target=run, daemon=True)
        thread.start()

"""
SOC Access Check Script (CLI Only)
-----------------------------------------
Checks a user's access across multiple SOC systems.

🛠️ Features:
- Runs system-specific access checks via external scripts.
- Logs results in Logs/SOC_Access_Log.txt.
- Automatically updates an RT ticket (if provided).
✅ **Designed for CLI operation only.** GUI is handled separately in soctool.py.
"""

import argparse
import logging

import subprocess
import sys
from datetime import datetime

# ✅ Ensure UTF-8 encoding (prevents UnicodeEncodeError)
sys.stdout.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")
sys.stderr.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")
sys.stdin.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")

# ✅ Set up base directories
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get current script location
UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils")  # Locate Utils folder
SYSTEMS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems")  # Locate Systems folder
LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Logs")  # Correct path to Logs/

# ✅ Ensure directories exist
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)  # Create Logs/ directory if missing
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.abspath(UTILS_DIR))  # Add Utils to Python path

# ✅ Attempt to import rt_api.py
try:
    from rt_api import add_comment  # Import RT API functionality
except ModuleNotFoundError as e:
    print(f"❌ Error: Could not import rt_api. Ensure 'Utils/' is inside 'soctool/' and properly structured.\n{e}")
    sys.exit(1)

# ✅ Set up logging
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "SOC_Access_Log.txt")
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s', level=logging.INFO)


def check_access(username, ldap_user, ldap_pass, rt_ticket=None):
    """
    Runs system-specific access checks and ensures output is correctly returned **only once**.
    """

    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    results = []  # Ensure we don't add the same line multiple times

    # ✅ Ensure log entry is only added once
    log_entry = f"🔹 Access check for {username} at {timestamp}"
    if log_entry not in results:
        results.append(log_entry)
        logging.info(log_entry)

    if not os.path.exists(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        error_msg = "❌ Error: 'Systems/' directory not found."
        results.append(error_msg)
        logging.error(error_msg)
        print("\n".join(results))
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return "\n".join(results)

    # ✅ Run each system check script only once
    for script in os.listdir(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        if script.endswith(".py"):  
            system_name = script.replace(".py", "").capitalize()
            script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)

            try:
                process = subprocess.Popen(
                    ["python", script_path, username],
                    stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
                    stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
                    text=True,
                    encoding="utf-8",
                    bufsize=1
                )

                stdout_output, stderr_output = process.communicate()

                if stdout_output.strip():
                    results.append(f"✅ {system_name}: {stdout_output.strip()}")
                    logging.info(f"{system_name} - {stdout_output.strip()}")

                if stderr_output.strip():
                    results.append(f"⚠️ {system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")
                    logging.error(f"{system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")

            except Exception as e:
                results.append(f"❌ {system_name}: Error running script - {e}")
                logging.error(f"Error running {system_name} script: {e}")

    summary = "\n".join(results)
    
    # ✅ Print once so soctool.py correctly captures it
    print(summary)
    sys.stdout.flush()
    
    return summary

if __name__ == "__main__":
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Check user access across SOC systems.")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_user", help="Your LDAP username")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_pass", help="Your LDAP password")
    parser.add_argument("username", help="LDAP username of the user to check")
    parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT Ticket number for documentation", nargs="?", default=None)

    args = parser.parse_args()

    # ✅ Call check_access only **once** and ensure it's printed correctly
    output = check_access(args.username, args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass, args.rt_ticket)
    print(output)  # ✅ Ensures output is captured by soctool.py







import logging
import psycopg2
import os
import subprocess
import sys

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ Dashlane CLI Path
DASHLANE_CLI_PATH = "C:\\Program Files\\DashlaneCLI\\dashlane.exe"

def get_dashlane_note(note_title):
    """Retrieve credentials stored in Dashlane Secure Note."""
    try:
        result = subprocess.run(
            [DASHLANE_CLI_PATH, "note", note_title],
            capture_output=True,
            text=True,
            check=True
        )

        lines = result.stdout.strip().split("\n")  # Split into lines
        if len(lines) < 2:
            logging.error("❌ Dashlane note does not contain expected credentials format!")
            return None, None

        return lines[0].strip(), lines[1].strip()  # Username, Password

    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to retrieve Dashlane note '{note_title}': {e}")
        return None, None

# ✅ Retrieve database credentials from Dashlane Secure Note
ADTRACK_DB_USER, ADTRACK_DB_PASS = get_dashlane_note("SOC - AdTrack Credentials")

DB_CONFIG = {
    "dbname": "adtrack_ro",
    "host": "vspool.som1.marchex.com",
    "port": 5432,
    "user": ADTRACK_DB_USER,
    "password": ADTRACK_DB_PASS
}

def get_db_connection():
    """Establish a database connection to AdTrack."""
    if not DB_CONFIG["user"] or not DB_CONFIG["password"]:
        logging.error("❌ Database credentials not found in Dashlane! Ensure Dashlane CLI is logged in.")
        return None

    try:
        return psycopg2.connect(**DB_CONFIG)
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Database connection failed: {e}")
        return None

def check_adtrack_access(user, vendor_email=None):
    """Check if a user has AdTrack UI access."""
    search_param = vendor_email or f"{user}@marchex.com"

    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        return None

    query = "SELECT email FROM at_user WHERE email ILIKE %s AND status != 'disabled'"
    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute(query, (search_param,))
            result = cur.fetchall()

        conn.close()
        return [row[0] for row in result] if result else None

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Database query failed: {e}")
        return None

def main():
    """Check AdTrack UI access and return results correctly."""
    
    user = input("Enter LDAP user to check: ").strip()
    is_vendor = input("Is this user a vendor? (Yes/No): ").strip().lower()
    vendor_email = input("Enter vendor email address: ") if is_vendor == "yes" else None

    access = check_adtrack_access(user, vendor_email)

    if access:
        result = f"✅ {user} has AdTrack UI access: {access}"
        logging.info(result)
    else:
        result = f"❌ {user} does NOT have AdTrack UI access."
        logging.info(result)

    # ✅ Ensure output prints correctly so it reaches checkaccess.py
    print(result)
    sys.stdout.flush()  # Ensures output is captured correctly

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

"""
SOC Access Check Script (CLI Only)
-----------------------------------------
Checks a user's access across multiple SOC systems.

🛠️ Features:
- Runs system-specific access checks via external scripts.
- Logs results in Logs/SOC_Access_Log.txt.
- Automatically updates an RT ticket (if provided).
✅ **Designed for CLI operation only.** GUI is handled separately in soctool.py.
"""

import argparse
import logging
import os
import subprocess
import sys
from datetime import datetime

# ✅ Ensure UTF-8 encoding (prevents UnicodeEncodeError)
sys.stdout.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")
sys.stderr.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")
sys.stdin.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")

# ✅ Set up base directories
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get current script location
UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils")  # Locate Utils folder
SYSTEMS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems")  # Locate Systems folder
LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Logs")  # Correct path to Logs/

# ✅ Ensure directories exist
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)  # Create Logs/ directory if missing
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.abspath(UTILS_DIR))  # Add Utils to Python path

# ✅ Attempt to import rt_api.py
try:
    from rt_api import add_comment  # Import RT API functionality
except ModuleNotFoundError as e:
    print(f"❌ Error: Could not import rt_api. Ensure 'Utils/' is inside 'soctool/' and properly structured.\n{e}")
    sys.exit(1)

# ✅ Set up logging
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "SOC_Access_Log.txt")
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s', level=logging.INFO)


def check_access(username, ldap_user, ldap_pass, rt_ticket=None):
    """
    Runs system-specific access checks and ensures output is correctly returned **only once**.
    """

    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    results = []  # Ensure we don't add the same line multiple times

    # ✅ Ensure log entry is only added once
    log_entry = f"🔹 Access check for {username} at {timestamp}"
    if log_entry not in results:
        results.append(log_entry)
        logging.info(log_entry)

    if not os.path.exists(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        error_msg = "❌ Error: 'Systems/' directory not found."
        results.append(error_msg)
        logging.error(error_msg)
        print("\n".join(results))
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return "\n".join(results)

    # ✅ Run each system check script only once
    for script in os.listdir(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        if script.endswith(".py"):  
            system_name = script.replace(".py", "").capitalize()
            script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)

            try:
                process = subprocess.Popen(
                    ["python", script_path, username],
                    stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
                    stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
                    text=True,
                    encoding="utf-8",
                    bufsize=1
                )

                # ✅ Capture both stdout and stderr in real time
                stdout_output, stderr_output = process.communicate()

                if stdout_output.strip():
                    results.append(f"✅ {system_name}: {stdout_output.strip()}")
                    logging.info(f"{system_name} - {stdout_output.strip()}")

                if stderr_output.strip():
                    results.append(f"⚠️ {system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")
                    logging.error(f"{system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")

            except Exception as e:
                results.append(f"❌ {system_name}: Error running script - {e}")
                logging.error(f"Error running {system_name} script: {e}")

    summary = "\n".join(results)
    
    # ✅ Print once so soctool.py correctly captures it
    print(summary)
    sys.stdout.flush()
    
    return summary


if __name__ == "__main__":

"""
SOC Access Granting Script (CLI Only)
-----------------------------------------
Grants access to a user across multiple SOC systems.

🛠️ Features:
- Runs system-specific grant scripts.
- Logs results in Logs/SOC_Access_Log.txt.
- Automatically updates an RT ticket (if provided).
✅ **Designed for CLI operation only.** GUI is handled separately in soctool.py.
"""

import argparse
import logging
import os
import subprocess
import sys
from datetime import datetime

# Ensure Utils is accessible for rt_api.py
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get current script location
UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "..", "Utils")  # Locate Utils folder
sys.path.append(UTILS_DIR)  # Add to system path

from rt_api import add_comment  # Import RT API functionality

# ✅ Define path to system grant scripts inside GrantAccess/Systems/
SYSTEMS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems")

# ✅ Ensure logs are stored in a Logs folder
LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "..", "Logs")
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)  # Create Logs directory if missing
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "SOC_Access_Log.txt")

# ✅ Configure logging format
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s', level=logging.INFO)

def grant_access(username, ldap_user, ldap_pass, mock_mode=False, rt_ticket=None):
    """
    Grants access to a user across multiple SOC systems.

    Args:
        username (str): The LDAP username to grant access to.
        ldap_user (str): The SOC user's LDAP username.
        ldap_pass (str): The SOC user's LDAP password.
        mock_mode (bool): Whether to run in mock mode (no real changes).
        rt_ticket (str, optional): RT ticket number for logging the access grant.

    Returns:
        None
    """

    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    logging.info(f"===== START: {timestamp} - Granting Access for {username} =====")

    results = []  # Store access grant results

    # Loop through all grant scripts in the Systems directory
    for script in os.listdir(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        if script.startswith("grant_") and script.endswith(".py"):
            system_name = script.replace("grant_", "").replace(".py", "").capitalize()
            script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)

            try:
                # Build the command for granting access
                cmd = ["python", script_path, username, "grant"]
                if mock_mode:
                    cmd.append("--mock")  # Append mock flag if enabled

                # Run the system-specific grant script
                result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True)

                # Append the result to the list
                results.append(f"✅ {system_name}: {result.stdout.strip()}")
                logging.info(f"{system_name} - {result.stdout.strip()}")

            except Exception as e:
                results.append(f"❌ {system_name}: Error running script - {e}")
                logging.error(f"Error running {system_name} script: {e}")

    # ✅ Summarize results
    summary = f"\n🔹 Access granted for {username} at {timestamp}\n" + "\n".join(results)

    # ✅ Log results to an RT ticket if provided
    if rt_ticket:
        add_comment(rt_ticket, summary)

    logging.info(f"===== END: {timestamp} - Granting Complete for {username} =====\n")

    # ✅ Print summary to CLI
    print(summary)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    # ✅ CLI Mode - Parse Command Line Arguments
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Grant user access across SOC systems.")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_user", help="Your LDAP username")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_pass", help="Your LDAP password")
    parser.add_argument("username", help="LDAP username of the user to grant access to")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode (no real changes)")
    parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT Ticket number for documentation", default=None)

    # Parse CLI arguments
    args = parser.parse_args()

    # Run the access grant function
    grant_access(args.username, args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass, args.mock, args.rt_ticket)




"""
SOC Access Removal Script (CLI Only)
-----------------------------------------
Removes access from a user across multiple SOC systems.

🛠️ Features:
- Runs system-specific removal scripts.
- Logs results in Logs/SOC_Access_Log.txt.
- Automatically updates an RT ticket (if provided).
✅ **Designed for CLI operation only.** GUI is handled separately in soctool.py.
"""

import argparse
import logging
import os
import subprocess
import sys
from datetime import datetime

# Ensure Utils is accessible for rt_api.py
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get current script location
UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "..", "Utils")  # Locate Utils folder
sys.path.append(UTILS_DIR)  # Add to system path

from rt_api import add_comment  # Import RT API functionality

# ✅ Define path to system removal scripts inside RemoveAccess/Systems/
SYSTEMS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems")

# ✅ Ensure logs are stored in a Logs folder
LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "..", "Logs")
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)  # Create Logs directory if missing
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "SOC_Access_Log.txt")

# ✅ Configure logging format
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s', level=logging.INFO)

def remove_access(username, ldap_user, ldap_pass, mock_mode=False, rt_ticket=None):
    """
    Removes access for a user across multiple SOC systems.

    Args:
        username (str): The LDAP username whose access is being removed.
        ldap_user (str): The SOC user's LDAP username.
        ldap_pass (str): The SOC user's LDAP password.
        mock_mode (bool): Whether to run in mock mode (no real changes).
        rt_ticket (str, optional): RT ticket number for logging the access removal.

    Returns:
        None
    """

    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    logging.info(f"===== START: {timestamp} - Removing Access for {username} =====")

    results = []  # Store access removal results

    # Loop through all remove scripts in the Systems directory
    for script in os.listdir(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        if script.startswith("remove_") and script.endswith(".py"):
            system_name = script.replace("remove_", "").replace(".py", "").capitalize()
            script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)

            try:
                # Build the command for removing access
                cmd = ["python", script_path, username, "remove"]
                if mock_mode:
                    cmd.append("--mock")  # Append mock flag if enabled

                # Run the system-specific remove script
                result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True)

                # Append the result to the list
                results.append(f"✅ {system_name}: {result.stdout.strip()}")
                logging.info(f"{system_name} - {result.stdout.strip()}")

            except Exception as e:
                results.append(f"❌ {system_name}: Error running script - {e}")
                logging.error(f"Error running {system_name} script: {e}")

    # ✅ Summarize results
    summary = f"\n🔹 Access removal for {username} at {timestamp}\n" + "\n".join(results)

    # ✅ Log results to an RT ticket if provided
    if rt_ticket:
        add_comment(rt_ticket, summary)

    logging.info(f"===== END: {timestamp} - Removal Complete for {username} =====\n")

    # ✅ Print summary to CLI
    print(summary)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    # ✅ CLI Mode - Parse Command Line Arguments
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Remove user access across SOC systems.")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_user", help="Your LDAP username")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_pass", help="Your LDAP password")
    parser.add_argument("username", help="LDAP username of the user to remove access from")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode (no real changes)")
    parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT Ticket number for documentation", default=None)

    # Parse CLI arguments
    args = parser.parse_args()

    # Run the access removal function
    remove_access(args.username, args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass, args.mock, args.rt_ticket)

"""
SOC Access Management Tool (CLI First, GUI Optional)
----------------------------------------------------
Provides a simple interface for SOC access management:
- Check User Access
- Grant User Access
- Remove User Access
- Clear RT Ticket Queue

🛠️ Designed for **command-line operation** with an optional GUI.
✅ Aligned with Matt's goal: **simplicity, maintainability, and clarity**.
"""

import sys
import os
import subprocess
import threading
import logging

# GUI Dependencies (Optional)
try:
    import tkinter as tk
    from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext
except ImportError:
    print("Tkinter is not installed. Run scripts via CLI instead.")
    sys.exit()

# Set up base directories
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get the script's directory
LOGS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Logs")
UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils")  # Locate utilities directory

# Ensure Logs directory exists
if not os.path.exists(LOGS_DIR):
    os.makedirs(LOGS_DIR)

# Add Utils directory to Python path for importing rt_api.py
sys.path.insert(0, UTILS_DIR)

# Import RT API functionality
try:
    from rt_api import add_comment
except ModuleNotFoundError as e:
    print(f"❌ Error: Could not import rt_api. Make sure Utils/ is in the correct location.\n{e}")
    sys.exit(1)

# Set up logging
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOGS_DIR, "soctool.log")
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, level=logging.INFO, format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s")

# Define paths to access management scripts
CHECK_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "checkaccess.py")
GRANT_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "grantaccess.py")
REMOVE_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "separation.py")
CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "close_cleared_rts.py")

# CLI Mode: Provide usage instructions
if len(sys.argv) > 1:
    print("\nSOC Access Management Tool (CLI First, GUI Optional)")
    print("====================================================")
    print("Usage:")
    print("  python soctool.py   # Starts the GUI (optional)")
    print("  python checkaccess.py <ldap_user> <ldap_pass> <target_user> --rt_ticket <ticket_number>")
    print("  python grantaccess.py <ldap_user> <ldap_pass> <target_user> --mock --rt_ticket <ticket_number>")
    print("  python separation.py <ldap_user> <ldap_pass> <target_user> --mock --rt_ticket <ticket_number>")
    print("  python close_cleared_rts.py   # Clears resolved RT tickets")
    sys.exit()  # Exit CLI mode

def execute_script(script_path, args, log_area):
    """Executes an external script **only once** and updates log output in the GUI."""

    def run():
        try:
            process = subprocess.Popen(
                ["python", script_path] + args,
                stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
                stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
                text=True,
                encoding="utf-8",
                bufsize=1
            )

            log_seen = set()  # ✅ Avoid duplicate log entries

            # ✅ Capture stdout and stderr in real-time
            for line in iter(process.stdout.readline, ""):
                line = line.strip()
                if line and line not in log_seen:
                    log_seen.add(line)
                    log_area.insert(tk.END, line + "\n")
                    log_area.see(tk.END)

            for line in iter(process.stderr.readline, ""):
                line = line.strip()
                if line and line not in log_seen:
                    log_seen.add(line)
                    log_area.insert(tk.END, f"⚠️ {line}\n")
                    log_area.see(tk.END)

            process.stdout.close()
            process.stderr.close()
            process.wait()

        except Exception as e:
            log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {str(e)}\n")
            logging.error(f"Error executing {script_path}: {str(e)}")

    # ✅ Ensure the thread runs only once
    if not threading.active_count() > 1:
        thread = threading.Thread(target=run, daemon=True)
        thread.start()




    
def open_access_window(action, script_path, show_mock_mode=True):
    """
    Opens a GUI window for user access management.

    Args:
        action (str): "Check", "Grant", or "Remove" (determines window title and action).
        script_path (str): Path to the corresponding script.
        show_mock_mode (bool): Whether to show the mock mode checkbox (only for Grant and Remove).
    """

    action_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    action_window.title(f"SOC - {action} Access")
    action_window.geometry("500x525")

    tk.Label(action_window, text=f"{action} User Access", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    # LDAP Credentials
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:").pack()
    ldap_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP password:").pack()
    ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40, show="*")  # Hide password input
    ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Target User
    tk.Label(action_window, text=f"Enter LDAP username to {action.lower()} access for:").pack()
    target_user_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    target_user_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # RT Ticket Number (Optional)
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter RT Ticket Number (Optional):").pack()
    rt_ticket_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    rt_ticket_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Mock Mode Toggle (only shown for Grant and Remove)
    mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=True)
    if show_mock_mode:
        tk.Checkbutton(action_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode).pack()

    # Log Display
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Logs:").pack()
    log_area = tk.Text(action_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    def execute_action(event=None):
        ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()
        ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()
        target_user = target_user_entry.get().strip()
        rt_ticket = rt_ticket_entry.get().strip() if rt_ticket_entry.get().strip() else None
        mock_flag = "--mock" if show_mock_mode and mock_mode.get() else ""

        if not ldap_user or not ldap_pass or not target_user:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "All fields are required except RT Ticket.")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Running {action} script for {target_user}...\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        # ✅ Properly format arguments
        args = [ldap_user, ldap_pass, target_user]
        if rt_ticket:
            args.extend(["--rt_ticket", rt_ticket])  # ✅ Add optional argument properly
        if mock_flag:
            args.append(mock_flag)

        execute_script(script_path, args, log_area)
        
    tk.Button(action_window, text="Execute", command=execute_action, font=("Arial", 12), width=20).pack(pady=10)
    action_window.bind("<Return>", execute_action)

def open_clear_rt_window():
    """
    Opens a GUI window to display RT queue clearing process in real-time.
    """

    rt_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    rt_window.title("Clearing RT Queue")
    rt_window.geometry("600x400")

    tk.Label(rt_window, text="Processing RT Queue...", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    # Log Display
    log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(rt_window, width=70, height=15)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    execute_script(CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT, [], log_area)

# GUI Window Setup
root = tk.Tk()
root.title("SOC Access Management")
root.geometry("400x350")
root.resizable(False, False)

# Header
tk.Label(root, text="SOC Access Management", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=20)

# Buttons to trigger scripts
tk.Button(root, text="Check User Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("Check", CHECK_ACCESS_SCRIPT, show_mock_mode=False), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Grant User Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("Grant", GRANT_ACCESS_SCRIPT, show_mock_mode=True), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Remove User Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("Remove", REMOVE_ACCESS_SCRIPT, show_mock_mode=True), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Clear RT Queue", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_clear_rt_window(), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

# Start GUI
root.mainloop()

from ldap3 import Server, Connection, ALL

LDAP_SERVERS = ["ldaps://10.90.255.145"]  # ✅ Secure LDAPS
LDAP_USERNAME = "CN=Kenneth Boller,OU=seattle,OU=users,OU=corp,DC=windows,DC=marchex,DC=com"
LDAP_PASSWORD = "$martLemur15"  # Replace with a secure storage method

for server_url in LDAP_SERVERS:
    try:
        print(f"🔍 Trying LDAP server: {server_url}")

        # ✅ Ensure SSL is used
        server = Server(server_url, get_info=ALL, use_ssl=True)

        # ✅ Try simple bind (CN format)
        try:
            print(f"🔄 Attempting SIMPLE BIND with username: {LDAP_USERNAME}")

            conn = Connection(
                server,
                user=LDAP_USERNAME,
                password=LDAP_PASSWORD,
                authentication="SIMPLE",
                auto_bind=True
            )

            if conn.bound:
                print(f"✅ Successfully authenticated to {server_url} as {LDAP_USERNAME}")
                break  # Exit on first successful connection

        except Exception as auth_error:
            print(f"⚠️ Failed SIMPLE BIND authentication: {auth_error}")

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ Error connecting to {server_url}: {e}")

print("🔍 LDAP Authentication test completed.")

from ldap3 import Server, Connection, ALL

LDAP_SERVERS = ["ldaps://10.90.255.145"]  # ✅ Secure LDAPS
LDAP_USERNAMES = [
    "CN=Kenneth Boller,OU=seattle,OU=users,OU=corp,DC=windows,DC=marchex,DC=com",  # Full DN ✅
    "kboller@windows.marchex.com",  # UPN ✅
    "windows\\kboller"  # NetBIOS (usually for NTLM)
]
LDAP_PASSWORD = "$martLemur15"  # Replace with a secure storage method

for server_url in LDAP_SERVERS:
    try:
        print(f"🔍 Trying LDAP server: {server_url}")

        # ✅ Ensure SSL is used
        server = Server(server_url, get_info=ALL, use_ssl=True)

        for username in LDAP_USERNAMES:
            try:
                print(f"🔄 Attempting SIMPLE BIND with username: {username}")

                conn = Connection(
                    server,
                    user=username,
                    password=LDAP_PASSWORD,
                    authentication="SIMPLE",
                    auto_bind=True
                )

                if conn.bound:
                    print(f"✅ Successfully authenticated to {server_url} as {username}")
                    exit()  # ✅ Exit script if successful

            except Exception as auth_error:
                print(f"⚠️ Failed authentication for {username}: {auth_error}")

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ Error connecting to {server_url}: {e}")

print("🔍 LDAP Authentication test completed.")

from ldap3 import Server, Connection, ALL, SIMPLE

LDAP_SERVERS = ["ldaps://10.90.255.145"]  # ✅ Secure LDAPS
LDAP_USERNAME = "CN=Kenneth Boller,OU=seattle,OU=users,OU=corp,DC=windows,DC=marchex,DC=com"
LDAP_PASSWORD = "$martLemur15"  # Secure properly

for server_url in LDAP_SERVERS:
    try:
        print(f"🔍 Trying LDAP server: {server_url}")

        # ✅ Ensure SSL is used
        server = Server(server_url, get_info=ALL, use_ssl=True)

        print(f"🔄 Attempting SIMPLE BIND with username: {LDAP_USERNAME}")

        conn = Connection(
            server,
            user=LDAP_USERNAME,
            password=LDAP_PASSWORD,
            authentication=SIMPLE,  # ✅ Using SIMPLE Bind
            auto_bind=True
        )

        if conn.bound:
            print(f"✅ Successfully authenticated to {server_url} as {LDAP_USERNAME}")
            exit()  # ✅ Exit script if successful

    except Exception as auth_error:
        print(f"⚠️ Failed authentication for {LDAP_USERNAME}: {auth_error}")

print("🔍 LDAP Authentication test completed.")

based off the names of the other key vaults, what should i name my key vault for this project and how should i create to match everyone elses so as not to raise concerns and questions and align with the rest of the company?
rather then moving forward with creating the key vault and the managed identity vm stuff today i think what id rather do is try to get thru each of the individual system scripts and make sure each script is complete and accurate per the SOP for access for each system, ill go ahead and send Matt a message asking for permissions and details on how he wants the SOC keyvault setup and if thats something he would even approve of and want me to do and in the mean time while we wait for a response from him lets get thru all the scripts and code them with that method of ldap authentication in mind, lets take a look at adtrack script and make sure it can check, grant and remove access and authenticate using azure key vault once the keyvault and managed identity is created for the adtrack db



import logging
import psycopg2
import os
import subprocess
import sys

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ Dashlane CLI Path
DASHLANE_CLI_PATH = "C:\\Program Files\\DashlaneCLI\\dashlane.exe"

def get_dashlane_note(note_title):
    """Retrieve credentials stored in Dashlane Secure Note."""
    try:
        result = subprocess.run(
            [DASHLANE_CLI_PATH, "note", note_title],
            capture_output=True,
            text=True,
            check=True
        )

        lines = result.stdout.strip().split("\n")  # Split into lines
        if len(lines) < 2:
            logging.error("❌ Dashlane note does not contain expected credentials format!")
            return None, None

        return lines[0].strip(), lines[1].strip()  # Username, Password

    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to retrieve Dashlane note '{note_title}': {e}")
        return None, None

# ✅ Retrieve database credentials from Dashlane Secure Note
ADTRACK_DB_USER, ADTRACK_DB_PASS = get_dashlane_note("SOC - AdTrack Credentials")

DB_CONFIG = {
    "dbname": "adtrack_ro",
    "host": "vspool.som1.marchex.com",
    "port": 5432,
    "user": ADTRACK_DB_USER,
    "password": ADTRACK_DB_PASS
}

def get_db_connection():
    """Establish a database connection to AdTrack."""
    if not DB_CONFIG["user"] or not DB_CONFIG["password"]:
        logging.error("❌ Database credentials not found in Dashlane! Ensure Dashlane CLI is logged in.")
        return None

    try:
        return psycopg2.connect(**DB_CONFIG)
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Database connection failed: {e}")
        return None

def check_adtrack_access(user, vendor_email=None):
    """Check if a user has AdTrack UI access."""
    search_param = vendor_email or f"{user}@marchex.com"

    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        error_msg = "❌ Database connection failed: Could not establish connection."
        logging.error(error_msg)
        print(error_msg)  # ✅ Ensure this prints so checkaccess.py captures it
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return None

    query = "SELECT email FROM at_user WHERE email ILIKE %s AND status != 'disabled'"
    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute(query, (search_param,))
            result = cur.fetchall()

        conn.close()

        if result:
            output = f"✅ {user} has AdTrack UI access: {result}"
        else:
            output = f"❌ {user} does NOT have AdTrack UI access."

        logging.info(output)
        print(output)  # ✅ Ensure this prints so it's visible in checkaccess.py
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return result

    except Exception as e:
        error_msg = f"❌ Database query failed: {e}"
        logging.error(error_msg)
        print(error_msg)  # ✅ Ensure errors are visible
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return None


def main():
    """Check AdTrack UI access and return results correctly."""
    
    user = input("Enter LDAP user to check: ").strip()
    is_vendor = input("Is this user a vendor? (Yes/No): ").strip().lower()
    vendor_email = input("Enter vendor email address: ") if is_vendor == "yes" else None

    access = check_adtrack_access(user, vendor_email)

    if access:
        result = f"✅ {user} has AdTrack UI access: {access}"
        logging.info(result)
    else:
        result = f"❌ {user} does NOT have AdTrack UI access."
        logging.info(result)

    # ✅ Ensure output prints correctly so it reaches checkaccess.py
    print(result)
    sys.stdout.flush()  # Ensures output is captured correctly

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

SOC SOP uiAccessAdTrack
