1	Description
2	Adding Access
2.1	If the user doesn't ask for "Staff level", email them asking them if they do and make sure to give them the URL for Adtrack Account standards to help them
2.1.1	NOTE
3	Removing Access
Description
This SOP is for adding and removing access for the Adtrack UI, aka Marchex.IO

Adding AccessRemoving Access

When an account needs to be added by request/ticket use the following steps.


If a user requests access to the Adtrack UI also called Marchex.io and need access to the tool. Most of our requests are for "staff level" access. See "Adtrack Account standards" link below

Adtrack Account standards 
If the user doesn't ask for "Staff level", email them asking them if they do and make sure to give them the URL for Adtrack Account standards to help them
http://wiki.marchex.com/index.php/SOC_SOP_adtrackUIAccountStandards

1. Log into Adtrack

Service Account & Password found in Bitwarden

2. Click the Client List tab in the UI.

3. Unless specified in the ticket create their account in the following group:

Marchex Voice Services (nee Voicestar) (This has been the historic place to put accounts for Marchex users.)

Note:

Sometimes you will have to match an account with another account.
The easiest way to do that is to open a two tabs in your browser.
In the first one, search in "Client list" using the target email (user to copy)
Then follow the below steps and just match up all the permissions.
4. Click on the Account Name, it will drop down, and click Account Settings.

5. Click Users

6. Click "New user".

7. Fill in the user's information:

Real Name
Email
Password [Password Gen]
NOTE:

If the email account is already in use, the tool will not let you use it again. You either have to alter the email with a Capital letter or find the other account and update that one.

8. Click submit at the bottom.

9. Search for the users account once more to provision it.

10. Using either given credentials from another account (Not preferred method) or [staff level] provision the account and click "update" at the bottom.

There are three specific pieces that Require more than the users manager approval: Bulk create /update Campaigns & accounts, Billing Write , and Edit Staff Permissions . See above staff level link.

11. Email the credentials to the user.


NOTE
Adtrack staff tools exist Here and will soon (hopefully) have a staff search function, at which point the above instructions will be thankfully obsolete.

Adding AccessRemoving Access

When an account needs to be removed either from a separation or SOX audit or team change use the following steps.


1. Log onto [AdtrackUI/Marchex.io]

Service Account & Password found in Keypass

2. Click on "Client List"

3. In the top right enter the email address of the user you wish to remove.

This will return account groups with the email addresses in the users.

4. For all account groups found, perform the following:

Click on the account, it will drop down. click Account Settings
Click Users
Search again in the top right corner for the user's email address
Click on the correct user
Click User Settings
Set the status to disabled
Click Update

since it is Monday and we are getting started up on this again after a long weekend away from it id like to take a look over each script and go over each one with a fine toothed comb and make sure each script is complete correct and accurate and meets matts guidelines, quoted below, and carrys out its intended functions starting with the gui script soctool. mock mode shuld be enabled by default for saftey and an RT ticket number should not be required but should be optional, if an RT ticket number is entered, a comment should be logged in that RT.
soctool.py is the gui version of the tool and is to be run by those that prefer gui and then the access_management.py script is the CLI version for those that prefer that method, the soctool script should call upon and use the access_management script and provide it with a GUI, soctool is not to be run with CLI and access_managment is not to have any GUI components.
soctool>access_management.py = GUI
access_management.py = CLI




Matt's guidelines: maintainability, simplicity, and clarity.


"A lot of these will probably have to be run on the SOC workstation from the command line in Azure so that it has access to the resources it needs.
I don't mind scripts that give access
But here's the thing, and this is what has gotten us in trouble and to this point, we want this simple and maintainable by anyone, not just you.
GUI adds complication
The scripts use to work great
Then Chelsea wanted a web UI...
Then Chelsea left the company without teaching anyone how to maintain it
We do not want to repeat these mistakes.
It's not so much that I have an affinity for CLI. I use to write web and GUI tools all of the time. The goal in this case is simplicity so that we never run into this again.
The first Callcap tool was something called the SITA Tool and it was written in VB6
I maintained it for YEARS
I wrote the original Callcap portal
And that was how I got away from VB6
Then I handed the portal off to other Devs
The issue with the SOC is that people write stuff and then don't had it off lol
So we're going for easy to understand and maintain
Because what seems simple now is not always simple later
It doesn't have to be the most basic stuff ever
But variable names should make sense and be description
And someone should be able to google the functions you use and understand them quickly
I know sometimes people will abstract things out with more advanced features, and that's fine, but then add a comment"






"""
SOC Access Management Tool (GUI)
----------------------------------------------------
✅ Optional GUI wrapper for access_management.py.
✅ LDAP authentication required before access actions.
✅ Calls access_management.py for check, grant, and remove actions.
"""

import sys
import os
import subprocess
import threading
import logging
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext

# ✅ Set up base directories
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get script directory
LOGS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Logs")
ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "access_management.py")  # New access management script

# ✅ Ensure Logs directory exists
os.makedirs(LOGS_DIR, exist_ok=True)

# ✅ Set up logging
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOGS_DIR, "soctool.log")
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, level=logging.INFO, format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s")

# ✅ Function to execute access management script
def execute_script(action, args, log_area):
    """Executes access_management.py and updates GUI log output."""

    def run():
        try:
            process = subprocess.Popen(
                ["python", ACCESS_SCRIPT, action] + args,
                stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
                stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
                text=True,
                encoding="utf-8",
                bufsize=1
            )

            for line in iter(process.stdout.readline, ""):
                log_area.insert(tk.END, line.strip() + "\n")
                log_area.see(tk.END)

            for line in iter(process.stderr.readline, ""):
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"⚠️ {line.strip()}\n")
                log_area.see(tk.END)

            process.stdout.close()
            process.stderr.close()
            process.wait()

        except Exception as e:
            log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {str(e)}\n")
            logging.error(f"Error executing {ACCESS_SCRIPT}: {str(e)}")

    thread = threading.Thread(target=run, daemon=True)
    thread.start()

# ✅ Function to open user access window
def open_access_window(action, show_mock_mode=True):
    """
    Opens GUI window for access management actions.
    Args:
        action (str): "check", "grant", or "remove".
        show_mock_mode (bool): Whether to show mock mode (for grant/remove).
    """

    action_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    action_window.title(f"SOC - {action.capitalize()} Access")
    action_window.geometry("500x525")

    tk.Label(action_window, text=f"{action.capitalize()} User Access", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Your LDAP Username:").pack()
    ldap_user_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    ldap_user_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Your LDAP Password:").pack()
    ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40, show="*")
    ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Target LDAP Username:").pack()
    target_user_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    target_user_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter RT Ticket Number (Optional):").pack()
    rt_ticket_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    rt_ticket_entry.pack(pady=5)

    mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=True)
    if show_mock_mode:
        tk.Checkbutton(action_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode).pack()

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Logs:").pack()
    log_area = tk.Text(action_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    def execute_action():
        ldap_user = ldap_user_entry.get().strip()
        ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()
        target_user = target_user_entry.get().strip()
        rt_ticket = rt_ticket_entry.get().strip() if rt_ticket_entry.get().strip() else None
        mock_flag = "--mock" if show_mock_mode and mock_mode.get() else ""

        if not ldap_user or not ldap_pass or not target_user:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "All fields are required.")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Running {action} access script for {target_user}...\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        args = [ldap_user, ldap_pass, target_user]
        if rt_ticket:
            args.extend(["--rt_ticket", rt_ticket])
        if mock_flag:
            args.append(mock_flag)

        execute_script(action, args, log_area)

    tk.Button(action_window, text="Execute", command=execute_action, font=("Arial", 12), width=20).pack(pady=10)

# ✅ Function to open RT queue clearing window
def open_clear_rt_window():
    """Opens a GUI window to display RT queue clearing process in real-time."""

    rt_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    rt_window.title("Clearing RT Queue")
    rt_window.geometry("600x400")

    tk.Label(rt_window, text="Processing RT Queue...", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(rt_window, width=70, height=15)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    execute_script("clear_rt", [], log_area)

# ✅ GUI Window Setup
root = tk.Tk()
root.title("SOC Access Management")
root.geometry("400x350")
root.resizable(False, False)

tk.Label(root, text="SOC Access Management", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=20)

tk.Button(root, text="Check User Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("check", show_mock_mode=False), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Grant User Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("grant", show_mock_mode=True), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Remove User Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("remove", show_mock_mode=True), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Clear RT Queue", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_clear_rt_window(), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

# ✅ Start GUI
root.mainloop()

perfect now lets look at the access_management.py script

"""
SOC Access Management Tool (CLI Only)
-----------------------------------------
Provides CLI-based access management for SOC:
- Check User Access
- Grant User Access
- Remove User Access

✅ CLI-first design for maintainability.
✅ Logs actions and optionally updates RT tickets.
✅ Independent from GUI (SOC Tool can call this script if needed).
"""
#Example CLI Usage
#python access_management.py check kboller
#python access_management.py grant kboller --rt_ticket 12345
#python access_management.py remove kboller --mock

import argparse
import logging
import os
import subprocess
import sys
from datetime import datetime
from ldap3 import Server, Connection, NTLM, ALL, core

# ✅ Ensure UTF-8 encoding to prevent errors
sys.stdout.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")
sys.stderr.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")

# ✅ Set up base directories
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get current script location
SYSTEMS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems")  # Locate Systems folder
LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Logs")  # Correct path to Logs/
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)  # Create Logs/ directory if missing

# ✅ Set up logging
LOGS_DIR = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)), "Logs")
os.makedirs(LOGS_DIR, exist_ok=True)
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOGS_DIR, "access_management.log")

logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, level=logging.INFO, format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s")

# ✅ Define LDAP Server Information
LDAP_SERVERS = ["ldap://ldap.oci-sjc-prd", "ldap://ldap.oci-iad-prd"]  # Both West & East
LDAP_DOMAIN = "YOURDOMAIN"  # Update with actual domain

# ✅ Attempt to import rt_api.py (for RT ticket updates)
try:
    sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils"))
    from rt_api import add_comment
except ModuleNotFoundError:
    def add_comment(ticket, comment):
        logging.warning(f"RT API not found. Skipping RT ticket update: {ticket}.")
        print(f"⚠️ RT API not found. Skipping RT ticket update: {ticket}.")

# ✅ Function to authenticate user via LDAP
def authenticate_ldap(username, password):
    """Authenticates the user against LDAP before allowing access management actions."""
    
    for server_url in LDAP_SERVERS:
        try:
            print(f"🔍 Trying LDAP server: {server_url}")
            server = Server(server_url, get_info=ALL)
            user_dn = f"{LDAP_DOMAIN}\\{username}"

            conn = Connection(server, user=user_dn, password=password, authentication=NTLM, auto_bind=True)

            if conn.bound:
                logging.info(f"✅ LDAP authentication successful for {username} on {server_url}")
                return True

        except core.exceptions.LDAPSocketOpenError:
            logging.warning(f"⚠️ Unable to connect to {server_url}. Trying next server...")

        except core.exceptions.LDAPBindError:
            logging.error(f"❌ Invalid LDAP credentials for {username}")
            print("Error: Invalid LDAP credentials.")
            return False

    logging.error("❌ All LDAP servers are unreachable.")
    print("Error: Unable to connect to any LDAP server.")
    return False

# ✅ Function to execute an access action
def manage_access(action, target_user, ldap_user, ldap_pass, rt_ticket=None, mock=False):
    """
    Executes access actions (check, grant, remove) after authenticating LDAP credentials.
    """
    if not authenticate_ldap(ldap_user, ldap_pass):
        print("❌ LDAP Authentication Failed. Access Denied.")
        sys.exit(1)

    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    results = [f"🔹 {action.capitalize()} access for {target_user} at {timestamp}"]

    # ✅ Define the path where system scripts are stored
    SYSTEMS_DIR = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)), "Systems")

    if not os.path.exists(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        results.append("❌ Error: 'Systems/' directory not found.")
        logging.error("Systems directory missing.")
        print("\n".join(results))
        sys.exit(1)

    # ✅ Run applicable system scripts
    for script in os.listdir(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        if script.endswith(".py") and script.startswith(action):
            system_name = script.replace(f"{action}_", "").replace(".py", "").capitalize()
            script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)

            try:
                cmd = ["python", script_path, target_user]
                if mock:
                    cmd.append("--mock")

                process = subprocess.Popen(cmd, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.PIPE, text=True, encoding="utf-8", bufsize=1)
                stdout_output, stderr_output = process.communicate()

                if stdout_output.strip():
                    results.append(f"✅ {system_name}: {stdout_output.strip()}")
                    logging.info(f"{system_name} - {stdout_output.strip()}")

                if stderr_output.strip():
                    results.append(f"⚠️ {system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")
                    logging.error(f"{system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")

            except Exception as e:
                results.append(f"❌ {system_name}: Error running script - {e}")
                logging.error(f"Error running {system_name} script: {e}")

    # ✅ Print final results
    print("\n".join(results))

# ✅ Function to execute system scripts
def execute_system_script(script_name, username, action, mock_mode=False):
    """
    Executes a system script for checking, granting, or removing user access.
    """

    script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script_name)
    if not os.path.exists(script_path):
        error_msg = f"❌ Error: {script_name} not found."
        logging.error(error_msg)
        print(error_msg)
        return error_msg

    try:
        cmd = ["python", script_path, username, action]
        if mock_mode:
            cmd.append("--mock")

        process = subprocess.Popen(
            cmd, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.PIPE, text=True, encoding="utf-8", bufsize=1
        )

        stdout_output, stderr_output = process.communicate()

        if stdout_output.strip():
            logging.info(f"{script_name}: {stdout_output.strip()}")
            print(stdout_output.strip())

        if stderr_output.strip():
            logging.error(f"{script_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")
            print(f"⚠️ {script_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")

        return stdout_output.strip() if stdout_output.strip() else stderr_output.strip()

    except Exception as e:
        error_msg = f"❌ {script_name}: Failed to execute - {e}"
        logging.error(error_msg)
        print(error_msg)
        return error_msg

# ✅ Function to check user access
def check_user_access(username):
    """Checks user access across SOC systems."""
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    print(f"🔹 Checking access for {username} at {timestamp}")
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {username}")

    # Run AdTrack Check
    return execute_system_script("adtrack.py", username, "check")

# ✅ Function to grant user access
def grant_user_access(username, mock_mode):
    """Grants access to a user."""
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    print(f"✅ Granting access to {username} at {timestamp}")
    logging.info(f"Granting access to {username}")

    # Run AdTrack Grant
    return execute_system_script("adtrack.py", username, "grant", mock_mode)

# ✅ Function to remove user access
def remove_user_access(username, mock_mode):
    """Removes user access."""
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    print(f"❌ Removing access for {username} at {timestamp}")
    logging.info(f"Removing access for {username}")

    # Run AdTrack Remove
    return execute_system_script("adtrack.py", username, "remove", mock_mode)

# ✅ Main function
if __name__ == "__main__":
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Manage SOC user access with LDAP authentication.")
    parser.add_argument("action", choices=["check", "grant", "remove"], help="Action to perform")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_user", help="Your LDAP username")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_pass", help="Your LDAP password")
    parser.add_argument("target_user", help="LDAP username of the target user")
    parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT Ticket number for documentation", default=None)
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode (for testing)")

    args = parser.parse_args()

    manage_access(args.action, args.target_user, args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass, args.rt_ticket, args.mock)

    if args.action == "check":
        result = check_user_access(args.username)
    elif args.action == "grant":
        result = grant_user_access(args.username, args.mock)
    elif args.action == "remove":
        result = remove_user_access(args.username, args.mock)

    # ✅ Log to RT Ticket if provided
    if args.rt_ticket and result:
        add_comment(args.rt_ticket, result)

"""
SOC Access Management Tool (CLI Only)
---------------------------------------------------
✅ CLI-based access management for SOC.
✅ Secure LDAP authentication via Azure Key Vault.
✅ Independent from GUI (SOC Tool calls this script).
"""

#Example CLI Usage
#python access_management.py check kboller
#python access_management.py grant kboller --rt_ticket 12345
#python access_management.py remove kboller --mock

import argparse
import logging
import os
import subprocess
import sys
from datetime import datetime
from ldap3 import Server, Connection, NTLM, ALL, core
from azure.identity import DefaultAzureCredential
from azure.keyvault.secrets import SecretClient

# ✅ Ensure UTF-8 encoding to prevent errors
sys.stdout.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")
sys.stderr.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")

# ✅ Set up base directories
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get current script location
SYSTEMS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems")  # Locate Systems folder
LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Logs")  # Correct path to Logs/
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)

# ✅ Set up logging
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "access_management.log")
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, level=logging.INFO, format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s")

# ✅ Azure Key Vault Configuration
KEY_VAULT_NAME = "soc-access-kv"  # Change if needed
KV_URI = f"https://{KEY_VAULT_NAME}.vault.azure.net/"
credential = DefaultAzureCredential()
kv_client = SecretClient(vault_url=KV_URI, credential=credential)

# ✅ Define LDAP Server
LDAP_SERVER = "ldaps://10.90.255.145"  # Update as needed

# ✅ Attempt to import rt_api.py (for RT ticket updates)
try:
    sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils"))
    from rt_api import add_comment
except ModuleNotFoundError:
    def add_comment(ticket, comment):
        logging.warning(f"RT API not found. Skipping RT ticket update: {ticket}.")
        print(f"⚠️ RT API not found. Skipping RT ticket update: {ticket}.")

# ✅ Retrieve Credentials from Azure Key Vault
def get_ldap_credentials():
    """Fetch LDAP credentials securely from Azure Key Vault."""
    try:
        ldap_user = kv_client.get_secret("ldap-username").value
        ldap_pass = kv_client.get_secret("ldap-password").value
        return ldap_user, ldap_pass
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to retrieve credentials from Key Vault: {e}")
        print("Error: Unable to retrieve credentials. Ensure Key Vault access is configured.")
        sys.exit(1)

# ✅ Function to authenticate via LDAP
def authenticate_ldap(username, password):
    """Authenticates against LDAP before proceeding with actions."""
    try:
        server = Server(LDAP_SERVER, get_info=None)
        conn = Connection(server, user=username, password=password, authentication=SIMPLE, auto_bind=AUTO_BIND_NO_TLS)
        return conn.bound
    except core.exceptions.LDAPBindError:
        logging.error(f"❌ Invalid LDAP credentials for {username}")
        print("Error: Invalid LDAP credentials.")
        return False
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ LDAP Connection Error: {e}")
        print("Error: Unable to connect to LDAP.")
        return False

# ✅ Centralized Execution of Access Actions
def manage_access(action, target_user, rt_ticket=None, mock=False):
    """
    Executes access actions (check, grant, remove) with LDAP authentication.
    """

    # ✅ Retrieve LDAP credentials securely
    ldap_user, ldap_pass = get_ldap_credentials()

    # ✅ Authenticate LDAP before proceeding
    if not authenticate_ldap(ldap_user, ldap_pass):
        print("❌ LDAP Authentication Failed. Access Denied.")
        sys.exit(1)

    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    results = [f"🔹 {action.capitalize()} access for {target_user} at {timestamp}"]

    # ✅ Ensure Systems Directory Exists
    if not os.path.exists(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        results.append("❌ Error: 'Systems/' directory not found.")
        logging.error("Systems directory missing.")
        print("\n".join(results))
        sys.exit(1)

    # ✅ Run applicable system scripts
    for script in os.listdir(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        if script.endswith(".py") and script.startswith(action):
            system_name = script.replace(f"{action}_", "").replace(".py", "").capitalize()
            script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)

            try:
                cmd = ["python", script_path, target_user]
                if mock:
                    cmd.append("--mock")

                process = subprocess.Popen(cmd, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.PIPE, text=True, encoding="utf-8", bufsize=1)
                stdout_output, stderr_output = process.communicate()

                if stdout_output.strip():
                    results.append(f"✅ {system_name}: {stdout_output.strip()}")
                    logging.info(f"{system_name} - {stdout_output.strip()}")

                if stderr_output.strip():
                    results.append(f"⚠️ {system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")
                    logging.error(f"{system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")

            except Exception as e:
                results.append(f"❌ {system_name}: Error running script - {e}")
                logging.error(f"Error running {system_name} script: {e}")

    # ✅ Print Final Results
    print("\n".join(results))


# ✅ CLI Argument Parsing
if __name__ == "__main__":
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Manage SOC user access with LDAP authentication.")
    parser.add_argument("action", choices=["check", "grant", "remove"], help="Action to perform")
    parser.add_argument("target_user", help="LDAP username of the target user")
    parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT Ticket number for documentation", default=None)
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode (for testing)")

    args = parser.parse_args()

    manage_access(args.action, args.target_user, args.rt_ticket, args.mock)
    
    # ✅ Log to RT Ticket if provided
    if args.rt_ticket and result:
        add_comment(args.rt_ticket, result)

"""
SOC Access Management Tool (CLI Only)
---------------------------------------------------
✅ CLI-based access management for SOC.
✅ Secure LDAP authentication via Azure Key Vault.
✅ Independent from GUI (SOC Tool calls this script).
"""

#Example CLI Usage
#python access_management.py check kboller
#python access_management.py grant kboller --rt_ticket 12345
#python access_management.py remove kboller --mock

import argparse
import logging
import os
import subprocess
import sys
from datetime import datetime
from ldap3 import Server, Connection, NTLM, ALL, core
from azure.identity import DefaultAzureCredential
from azure.keyvault.secrets import SecretClient

# ✅ Ensure UTF-8 encoding to prevent errors
sys.stdout.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")
sys.stderr.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")

# ✅ Set up base directories
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get current script location
SYSTEMS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems")  # Locate Systems folder
LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Logs")  # Correct path to Logs/
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)

# ✅ Set up logging
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "access_management.log")
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, level=logging.INFO, format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s")

# ✅ Azure Key Vault Configuration
KEY_VAULT_NAME = "soc-access-kv"  # Change if needed
KV_URI = f"https://{KEY_VAULT_NAME}.vault.azure.net/"
credential = DefaultAzureCredential()
kv_client = SecretClient(vault_url=KV_URI, credential=credential)

# ✅ Define LDAP Server
LDAP_SERVER = "ldaps://10.90.255.145"  # Update as needed

# ✅ Attempt to import rt_api.py (for RT ticket updates)
try:
    sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils"))
    from rt_api import add_comment
except ModuleNotFoundError:
    def add_comment(ticket, comment):
        logging.warning(f"RT API not found. Skipping RT ticket update: {ticket}.")
        print(f"⚠️ RT API not found. Skipping RT ticket update: {ticket}.")

# ✅ Retrieve Credentials from Azure Key Vault
def get_ldap_credentials():
    """Fetch LDAP credentials securely from Azure Key Vault."""
    try:
        ldap_user = kv_client.get_secret("ldap-username").value
        ldap_pass = kv_client.get_secret("ldap-password").value
        return ldap_user, ldap_pass
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to retrieve credentials from Key Vault: {e}")
        print("Error: Unable to retrieve credentials. Ensure Key Vault access is configured.")
        sys.exit(1)

# ✅ Function to authenticate via LDAP
def authenticate_ldap(username, password):
    """Authenticates against LDAP before proceeding with actions."""
    try:
        server = Server(LDAP_SERVER, get_info=None)
        conn = Connection(server, user=username, password=password, authentication=SIMPLE, auto_bind=AUTO_BIND_NO_TLS)
        return conn.bound
    except core.exceptions.LDAPBindError:
        logging.error(f"❌ Invalid LDAP credentials for {username}")
        print("Error: Invalid LDAP credentials.")
        return False
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ LDAP Connection Error: {e}")
        print("Error: Unable to connect to LDAP.")
        return False


# ✅ Prompt for missing inputs
def prompt_if_missing(value, prompt_text):
    """Prompt user for input if a value is missing."""
    return value if value else input(prompt_text).strip()


# ✅ Centralized Execution of Access Actions
def manage_access(action=None, target_user=None, rt_ticket=None, mock=False):
    """
    Executes access actions (check, grant, remove) with LDAP authentication.
    Prompts user for missing arguments if not provided via CLI.
    """

    # ✅ Prompt for missing inputs
    action = prompt_if_missing(action, "Enter action (check/grant/remove): ").lower()
    while action not in ["check", "grant", "remove"]:
        print("❌ Invalid action. Please enter 'check', 'grant', or 'remove'.")
        action = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter action (check/grant/remove): ").lower()

    target_user = prompt_if_missing(target_user, "Enter the LDAP username of the target user: ")

    if action in ["grant", "remove"]:
        rt_ticket = prompt_if_missing(rt_ticket, "Enter RT Ticket Number (Optional, press Enter to skip): ")

    # ✅ Retrieve LDAP credentials securely
    ldap_user, ldap_pass = get_ldap_credentials()

    # ✅ Authenticate LDAP before proceeding
    if not authenticate_ldap(ldap_user, ldap_pass):
        print("❌ LDAP Authentication Failed. Access Denied.")
        sys.exit(1)

    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    results = [f"🔹 {action.capitalize()} access for {target_user} at {timestamp}"]

    # ✅ Ensure Systems Directory Exists
    if not os.path.exists(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        results.append("❌ Error: 'Systems/' directory not found.")
        logging.error("Systems directory missing.")
        print("\n".join(results))
        sys.exit(1)

    # ✅ Run applicable system scripts
    for script in os.listdir(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        if script.endswith(".py") and script.startswith(action):
            system_name = script.replace(f"{action}_", "").replace(".py", "").capitalize()
            script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)

            try:
                cmd = ["python", script_path, target_user]
                if mock:
                    cmd.append("--mock")

                process = subprocess.Popen(cmd, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.PIPE, text=True, encoding="utf-8", bufsize=1)
                stdout_output, stderr_output = process.communicate()

                if stdout_output.strip():
                    results.append(f"✅ {system_name}: {stdout_output.strip()}")
                    logging.info(f"{system_name} - {stdout_output.strip()}")

                if stderr_output.strip():
                    results.append(f"⚠️ {system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")
                    logging.error(f"{system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")

            except Exception as e:
                results.append(f"❌ {system_name}: Error running script - {e}")
                logging.error(f"Error running {system_name} script: {e}")

    # ✅ Print Final Results
    print("\n".join(results))

    # ✅ Log to RT Ticket if provided
    if rt_ticket:
        add_comment(rt_ticket, "\n".join(results))

# ✅ CLI Argument Parsing
if __name__ == "__main__":
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Manage SOC user access with LDAP authentication.")
    parser.add_argument("action", nargs="?", choices=["check", "grant", "remove"], help="Action to perform (check, grant, remove)")
    parser.add_argument("target_user", nargs="?", help="LDAP username of the target user")
    parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT Ticket number for documentation", default=None)
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode (for testing)")

    args = parser.parse_args()

    # ✅ Call manage_access() with the parsed arguments, allowing missing inputs to be prompted
    manage_access(args.action, args.target_user, args.rt_ticket, args.mock)

"""
SOC Access Management Tool (CLI Only)
---------------------------------------------------
✅ CLI-based access management for SOC.
✅ Secure LDAP authentication via Azure Key Vault.
✅ Interactive access management (Check → Remove/Grant).
✅ Independent from GUI (SOC Tool calls this script).
"""

#Example CLI Usage
#python access_management.py check kboller
#python access_management.py grant kboller --rt_ticket 12345
#python access_management.py remove kboller --mock

import argparse
import logging
import os
import subprocess
import sys
from datetime import datetime
from ldap3 import Server, Connection, NTLM, ALL, core
from azure.identity import DefaultAzureCredential
from azure.keyvault.secrets import SecretClient

# ✅ Ensure UTF-8 encoding to prevent errors
sys.stdout.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")
sys.stderr.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")

# ✅ Set up base directories
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get current script location
SYSTEMS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems")  # Locate Systems folder
LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Logs")  # Correct path to Logs/
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)

# ✅ Set up logging
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "access_management.log")
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, level=logging.INFO, format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s")

# ✅ Azure Key Vault Configuration
KEY_VAULT_NAME = "soc-access-kv"  # Change if needed
KV_URI = f"https://{KEY_VAULT_NAME}.vault.azure.net/"
credential = DefaultAzureCredential()
kv_client = SecretClient(vault_url=KV_URI, credential=credential)

# ✅ Define LDAP Server
LDAP_SERVER = "ldaps://10.90.255.145"  # Update as needed

# ✅ Attempt to import rt_api.py (for RT ticket updates)
try:
    sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils"))
    from rt_api import add_comment
except ModuleNotFoundError:
    def add_comment(ticket, comment):
        logging.warning(f"RT API not found. Skipping RT ticket update: {ticket}.")
        print(f"⚠️ RT API not found. Skipping RT ticket update: {ticket}.")

# ✅ Retrieve Credentials from Azure Key Vault
def get_ldap_credentials():
    """Fetch LDAP credentials securely from Azure Key Vault."""
    try:
        ldap_user = kv_client.get_secret("ldap-username").value
        ldap_pass = kv_client.get_secret("ldap-password").value
        return ldap_user, ldap_pass
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to retrieve credentials from Key Vault: {e}")
        print("Error: Unable to retrieve credentials. Ensure Key Vault access is configured.")
        sys.exit(1)

# ✅ Function to authenticate via LDAP
def authenticate_ldap(username, password):
    """Authenticates against LDAP before proceeding with actions."""
    try:
        server = Server(LDAP_SERVER, get_info=None)
        conn = Connection(server, user=username, password=password, authentication=SIMPLE, auto_bind=AUTO_BIND_NO_TLS)
        return conn.bound
    except core.exceptions.LDAPBindError:
        logging.error(f"❌ Invalid LDAP credentials for {username}")
        print("Error: Invalid LDAP credentials.")
        return False
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ LDAP Connection Error: {e}")
        print("Error: Unable to connect to LDAP.")
        return False


# ✅ Prompt for missing inputs
def prompt_if_missing(value, prompt_text):
    """Prompt user for input if a value is missing."""
    return value if value else input(prompt_text).strip()


# ✅ Check user access
def check_user_access(target_user):
    """Checks all systems where the user has access."""
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    print(f"🔹 Checking access for {target_user} at {timestamp}")
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {target_user}")

    access_list = []

    for script in os.listdir(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        if script.endswith(".py") and script.startswith("check_"):
            system_name = script.replace("check_", "").replace(".py", "").capitalize()
            script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)

            try:
                cmd = ["python", script_path, target_user]
                process = subprocess.Popen(cmd, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.PIPE, text=True, encoding="utf-8", bufsize=1)
                stdout_output, stderr_output = process.communicate()

                if stdout_output.strip():
                    print(f"✅ {system_name}: {stdout_output.strip()}")
                    access_list.append(system_name)

                if stderr_output.strip():
                    print(f"⚠️ {system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")
                    logging.error(f"{system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")

            except Exception as e:
                print(f"❌ {system_name}: Error checking access - {e}")
                logging.error(f"Error checking access for {system_name}: {e}")

    return access_list

# ✅ Remove access from a system
def remove_access(target_user, system_name):
    """Removes access from the selected system."""
    script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, f"remove_{system_name.lower()}.py")

    if os.path.exists(script_path):
        cmd = ["python", script_path, target_user]
        subprocess.run(cmd, text=True, encoding="utf-8")
        print(f"✅ Removed access to {system_name} for {target_user}")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Remove script for {system_name} not found.")

# ✅ Grant access to a system
def grant_access(target_user, system_name):
    """Grants access to the selected system."""
    script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, f"grant_{system_name.lower()}.py")

    if os.path.exists(script_path):
        cmd = ["python", script_path, target_user]
        subprocess.run(cmd, text=True, encoding="utf-8")
        print(f"✅ Granted access to {system_name} for {target_user}")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Grant script for {system_name} not found.")

# ✅ Main interactive workflow
def interactive_access_management():
    """Runs the interactive access management process."""

    # ✅ Retrieve LDAP credentials securely
    ldap_user, ldap_pass = get_ldap_credentials()

    # ✅ Authenticate LDAP before proceeding
    if not authenticate_ldap(ldap_user, ldap_pass):
        print("❌ LDAP Authentication Failed. Access Denied.")
        sys.exit(1)

    # ✅ Get the target LDAP username
    target_user = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the LDAP username of the target user: ")

    # ✅ Check access first
    access_list = check_user_access(target_user)

    if access_list:
        print("\n🔹 The user currently has access to these systems:")
        for i, system in enumerate(access_list, start=1):
            print(f"  {i}. {system}")

        # ✅ Ask if access should be removed
        remove_choice = input("\nWould you like to remove access from any of these systems? (yes/no): ").strip().lower()
        if remove_choice == "yes":
            system_to_remove = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the system name to remove access from: ")
            if system_to_remove in access_list:
                remove_access(target_user, system_to_remove)
            else:
                print("❌ Invalid selection. System not found in the access list.")

    # ✅ Ask if access should be granted
    grant_choice = input("\nWould you like to grant access to a new system? (yes/no): ").strip().lower()
    if grant_choice == "yes":
        system_to_grant = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the system name to grant access to: ")
        grant_access(target_user, system_to_grant)

    print("\n🔹 Access management completed.")

# ✅ Run the interactive workflow if script is run without CLI arguments
if __name__ == "__main__":
    interactive_access_management()

import logging
import subprocess
import shutil
import json

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

def check_aws_cli():
    """Check if AWS CLI is installed."""
    if not shutil.which("aws"):
        logging.error("AWS CLI is not installed. Please install it using 'pip install awscli'.")
        return False
    return True

def get_aws_users(auth_user, mock_mode):
    """Retrieve the list of AWS IAM users."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info("[MOCK] Simulating AWS IAM user list retrieval.")
        return {"mockuser1", "mockuser2", "mockadmin"}  # Simulated AWS users

    try:
        output = subprocess.check_output(['aws', 'iam', 'list-users', '--profile', auth_user], stderr=subprocess.STDOUT)
        users = json.loads(output).get('Users', [])
        return {user['UserName'] for user in users}
    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
        logging.error(f"AWS CLI error: {e.output.decode().strip()}")
        return None

def main(user, creds):
    """Check if a user has AWS IAM access."""
    mock_mode = creds["MOCK_MODE"]  # Read Mock Mode from creds

    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Checking AWS IAM access for {user}.")
        return (user, user, creds) if user in {"mockuser1", "mockuser2", "mockadmin"} else (None, user, creds)

    if not check_aws_cli():
        return None, user, creds

    auth_user = creds['operatorUN']
    aws_users = get_aws_users(auth_user, mock_mode)

    if aws_users is None:
        return None, user, creds

    return (user, user, creds) if user in aws_users else (None, user, creds)

def foundAccess(result):
    """Check if the user has AWS IAM access and remove if required."""
    if result[0]:
        user = result[1]
        accessChoice = result[2]['accessChoice']
        mock_mode = result[2]["MOCK_MODE"]

        if accessChoice == "check":
            logging.info(f"{user} has AWS IAM access.")
        elif accessChoice == "remove":
            logging.info(f"{user} has AWS IAM access. Attempting removal...")
            deleteAccess(user, result[2]['operatorUN'], mock_mode)

def deleteAccess(user, auth_user, mock_mode):
    """Remove AWS IAM access for a given user."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would remove AWS IAM access for {user}.")
        return  # Skip actual deletion in mock mode

    try:
        subprocess.check_output(['aws', 'iam', 'delete-user', '--profile', auth_user, '--user-name', user], stderr=subprocess.STDOUT)
        logging.info(f"AWS IAM access removed for {user}.")
    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to remove AWS IAM access for {user}: {e.output.decode().strip()}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    logging.info("Checking AWS IAM access...")

    operatorUN = input("Enter your LDAP username: ").strip()
    users = input("Enter username(s) to check (comma-separated): ").strip().split(",")
    accessChoice = input("Would you like to check or remove access? (Check/Remove): ").strip().lower()

    while accessChoice not in ("remove", "check"):
        accessChoice = input("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check': ").strip().lower()

    creds = {
        "operatorUN": operatorUN,
        "accessChoice": accessChoice,
        "MOCK_MODE": True  # This would be overridden when called from separations.py
    }

    for user in users:
        result = main(user.strip(), creds)
        foundAccess(result)

Description
This SOP is for adding and removing access for the AWS.

Here is a note on AWS and sub accounts [Cross Account Access].
IAM logins need to first authenticate to the infrastructure-aws account, then if they need and already HAVE the access they can flip to a different sub account.
The MIND+ Team has their own account. If someone is asking for access to it, see [This Wiki]


Adding User AccessAdding Application User(OLD) Attach Users to Queues(NEW) Attach Users to QueuesCreating Finance Team IAM UserRemoving Access



User Access
1. Go the AWS and login https://console.aws.amazon.com/

2. Typing IAM in the search box

3. Click users at the left side

4. Searching the username(email) you want to create, if it’s not existing clicking “Add user” to create it.

5. Typing the username(email), in the access type choose “AWS Management Console access” then using autogenerated password and check “Users must create a new password at next sign-in” after all, go the “next Permissions“

6. When you go to next screen. Click second box “Copy permissions from existing user”. Searching the name you got from ticket and select it

Tips: you should find the name which we need copy from in the request ticket, if not you should send Email to his/her manager to ask.

7. After all, click the Review and checking all the information. Then click “create user”

8. 8. Send the password to user following the requirements below.

If the user has a Marchex.com email use that. If they don't, then use Slack or Teams.
NOTE: do NOT send the password over email if it is not an @marchex.com email - use Slack or Teams


Modifying Policies and arns
Sometimes you'll get a ticket like this one that infra used to do, but we'll do it now.
1. There's a lot of grey area here, sorry
2. Go here
3. If the ticket is like the above, and they show you the permissions they have and the permissions they need, follow the bullets in this step. Otherwise go to step 4.

Click "Users" on the left, search for the user you need, and click on their email address
Under "Policy Name", expand all policies
Search for the arn that they have, so you can find the policy that needs to be updated. In the above example, if you look in the policy "MarchexDSEngPolicy", you will be able to see the resource group.
Click on "Edit Policy", and move to step 5
4. If the ticket is asking to add an arn to a specific group, you should use the bullets in this step.

Click "Policies" on the left, Search for the policy you want, and click on it
Click on "Edit Policy" and move to step 5.
5. Click on the JSON tab
6. Find the sections that have other arns in the "Resource" block that match the desired arn

For example, if the desired arn is "arn:aws:elasticloadbalancing:*:111781987845:loadbalancer/app/ds-*", you'd put it in a block or blocks that has elasticloadbalancing as the Action, with similar Resources.

7. Click "Review Policy", and "Save Policy"



I Can't Create an SQS
If the ticket is like this one and they're asking to have access to make an SQS, this is the place for you
1. Make sure the ticket includes the team or product owner they're a member of. In the case above, Rajan is a member of the MC2 team

2. Go here, and type in something that you could match an AWS group to the team with. In the example above, I typed in "mc2" and the group "mchx-aim-mc2" came up.

3. Click on the best match for what you're looking for. There is not a good way to tell you which one to click on in an SOP, so if you're unsure you should ask someone, or just use your best judgement.

4. Click "Add user to group", and add the user requesting access

SOC SOP uiAccessAWS
SOC SOP uiAccessAWS

3.1	This will be a ticket that looks a lot like this

6	Creating Finance Team IAM User
6.1	This will be a ticket that looks a lot like this
7	Removing Access
Description
This SOP is for adding and removing access for the AWS.

Here is a note on AWS and sub accounts [Cross Account Access].
IAM logins need to first authenticate to the infrastructure-aws account, then if they need and already HAVE the access they can flip to a different sub account.
The MIND+ Team has their own account. If someone is asking for access to it, see [This Wiki]


Adding User AccessAdding Application User(OLD) Attach Users to Queues(NEW) Attach Users to QueuesCreating Finance Team IAM UserRemoving Access

1. Go the AWS and login https://console.aws.amazon.com/

2. Typing IAM in the search box

3. Click users at the left side

4. Searching the username(email) you want to delete, select it and click Delete User .

mock mode for the aws.py script should be toggled from either the soctool.py script (GUI) or the access_management.py script (CLI) not within the AWS.py script.
all of the individual system script (adtrack.py, aws.py) are located in SOCTool/Systems/UIs/ when running the access_management.py script once the user inputs the target users ldap username the access_management.py script should call each of the scripts in the Systems/UIs/ directory and check target users access to each system using the check access function from each system script and output the results of which systems the target ldap user has access to.




"""
SOC Access Management Tool (CLI Only)
---------------------------------------------------
✅ CLI-based access management for SOC.
✅ Secure LDAP authentication via Azure Key Vault.
✅ Interactive access management (Check → Remove/Grant).
✅ Independent from GUI (SOC Tool calls this script).
"""

#Example CLI Usage
#python access_management.py check kboller
#python access_management.py grant kboller --rt_ticket 12345
#python access_management.py remove kboller --mock

import argparse
import logging
import os
import subprocess
import sys
from datetime import datetime
from ldap3 import Server, Connection, NTLM, ALL, core
#from azure.identity import DefaultAzureCredential
#from azure.keyvault.secrets import SecretClient

# ✅ Ensure UTF-8 encoding to prevent errors
sys.stdout.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")
sys.stderr.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")

# ✅ Set up base directories
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get current script location
SYSTEMS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems")  # Locate Systems folder
LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Logs")  # Correct path to Logs/
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)

# ✅ Set up logging
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "access_management.log")
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, level=logging.INFO, format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s")

# ✅ Azure Key Vault Configuration
#KEY_VAULT_NAME = "soc-access-kv"  # Change if needed
#KV_URI = f"https://{KEY_VAULT_NAME}.vault.azure.net/"
#credential = DefaultAzureCredential()
#kv_client = SecretClient(vault_url=KV_URI, credential=credential)

# ✅ Define LDAP Server
#LDAP_SERVER = "ldaps://10.90.255.145"  # Update as needed

# ✅ Attempt to import rt_api.py (for RT ticket updates)
try:
    sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils"))
    from rt_api import add_comment
except ModuleNotFoundError:
    def add_comment(ticket, comment):
        logging.warning(f"RT API not found. Skipping RT ticket update: {ticket}.")
        print(f"⚠️ RT API not found. Skipping RT ticket update: {ticket}.")

# ✅ Retrieve Credentials from Azure Key Vault
#def get_ldap_credentials():
#    """Fetch LDAP credentials securely from Azure Key Vault."""
#    try:
#        ldap_user = kv_client.get_secret("ldap-username").value
#        ldap_pass = kv_client.get_secret("ldap-password").value
#        return ldap_user, ldap_pass
#    except Exception as e:
#        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to retrieve credentials from Key Vault: {e}")
#        print("Error: Unable to retrieve credentials. Ensure Key Vault access is configured.")
#        sys.exit(1)

# ✅ Function to authenticate via LDAP
#def authenticate_ldap(username, password):
#    """Authenticates against LDAP before proceeding with actions."""
#    try:
#        server = Server(LDAP_SERVER, get_info=None)
#        conn = Connection(server, user=username, password=password, authentication=SIMPLE, auto_bind=AUTO_BIND_NO_TLS)
#        return conn.bound
#    except core.exceptions.LDAPBindError:
#        logging.error(f"❌ Invalid LDAP credentials for {username}")
#        print("Error: Invalid LDAP credentials.")
#        return False
#    except Exception as e:
#        logging.error(f"❌ LDAP Connection Error: {e}")
#        print("Error: Unable to connect to LDAP.")
#        return False


# ✅ Simulated LDAP Authentication for Testing
def authenticate_ldap(username, password):
    """Simulated LDAP authentication (Always returns True for testing)."""
    print(f"✅ Simulated LDAP authentication successful for {username}.")
    return True  # Always return True for testing


# ✅ Prompt for missing inputs
def prompt_if_missing(value, prompt_text):
    """Prompt user for input if a value is missing."""
    return value if value else input(prompt_text).strip()


# ✅ Check user access
def check_user_access(target_user):
    """Checks all systems where the user has access."""
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    print(f"🔹 Checking access for {target_user} at {timestamp}")
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {target_user}")

    access_list = []

    for script in os.listdir(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        if script.endswith(".py") and script.startswith("check_"):
            system_name = script.replace("check_", "").replace(".py", "").capitalize()
            script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)

            try:
                cmd = ["python", script_path, target_user]
                process = subprocess.Popen(cmd, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.PIPE, text=True, encoding="utf-8", bufsize=1)
                stdout_output, stderr_output = process.communicate()

                if stdout_output.strip():
                    print(f"✅ {system_name}: {stdout_output.strip()}")
                    access_list.append(system_name)

                if stderr_output.strip():
                    print(f"⚠️ {system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")
                    logging.error(f"{system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")

            except Exception as e:
                print(f"❌ {system_name}: Error checking access - {e}")
                logging.error(f"Error checking access for {system_name}: {e}")

    return access_list

# ✅ Remove access from a system
def remove_access(target_user, system_name):
    """Removes access from the selected system."""
    script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, f"remove_{system_name.lower()}.py")

    if os.path.exists(script_path):
        cmd = ["python", script_path, target_user]
        subprocess.run(cmd, text=True, encoding="utf-8")
        print(f"✅ Removed access to {system_name} for {target_user}")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Remove script for {system_name} not found.")

# ✅ Grant access to a system
def grant_access(target_user, system_name):
    """Grants access to the selected system."""
    script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, f"grant_{system_name.lower()}.py")

    if os.path.exists(script_path):
        cmd = ["python", script_path, target_user]
        subprocess.run(cmd, text=True, encoding="utf-8")
        print(f"✅ Granted access to {system_name} for {target_user}")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Grant script for {system_name} not found.")

# ✅ Main interactive workflow
def interactive_access_management():
    """Runs the interactive access management process."""

    # ✅ Simulate LDAP Credentials Instead of Fetching from Key Vault
    ldap_user = "mock_user@company.com"
    ldap_pass = "mock_password"

    # ✅ Retrieve LDAP credentials securely
    #ldap_user, ldap_pass = get_ldap_credentials()

    # ✅ Authenticate LDAP before proceeding
    if not authenticate_ldap(ldap_user, ldap_pass):
        print("❌ LDAP Authentication Failed. Access Denied.")
        sys.exit(1)

    # ✅ Get the target LDAP username
    target_user = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the LDAP username of the target user: ")

    # ✅ Check access first
    access_list = check_user_access(target_user)

    if access_list:
        print("\n🔹 The user currently has access to these systems:")
        for i, system in enumerate(access_list, start=1):
            print(f"  {i}. {system}")

        # ✅ Ask if access should be removed
        remove_choice = input("\nWould you like to remove access from any of these systems? (yes/no): ").strip().lower()
        if remove_choice == "yes":
            system_to_remove = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the system name to remove access from: ")
            if system_to_remove in access_list:
                remove_access(target_user, system_to_remove)
            else:
                print("❌ Invalid selection. System not found in the access list.")

    # ✅ Ask if access should be granted
    grant_choice = input("\nWould you like to grant access to a new system? (yes/no): ").strip().lower()
    if grant_choice == "yes":
        system_to_grant = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the system name to grant access to: ")
        grant_access(target_user, system_to_grant)

    print("\n🔹 Access management completed.")

# ✅ Run the interactive workflow if script is run without CLI arguments
if __name__ == "__main__":
    interactive_access_management()
"""
SOC Access Management Tool (CLI Only)
---------------------------------------------------
✅ CLI-based access management for SOC.
✅ Secure LDAP authentication via Azure Key Vault.
✅ Interactive access management (Check → Remove/Grant).
✅ Independent from GUI (SOC Tool calls this script).
"""

LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "access_management.log")
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, level=logging.INFO, format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s")

except ModuleNotFoundError:

# ✅ Simulated LDAP Authentication for Testing
def authenticate_ldap(username, password):
    """Simulated LDAP authentication (Always returns True for testing)."""
    print(f"✅ Simulated LDAP authentication successful for {username}.")
    return True  # Always return True for testing


# ✅ Prompt for missing inputs
def prompt_if_missing(value, prompt_text):
    """Prompt user for input if a value is missing."""
    return value if value else input(prompt_text).strip()


# ✅ Check user access
def check_user_access(target_user):
    """Checks all systems where the user has access."""
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    print(f"🔹 Checking access for {target_user} at {timestamp}")
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {target_user}")

    access_list = []

    if not os.path.exists(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        print("❌ Error: 'Systems/UIs' directory not found.")
        logging.error("Systems directory missing.")
        sys.exit(1)


    for script in os.listdir(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        if script.endswith(".py") and script.startswith("check_"):
            system_name = script.replace("check_", "").replace(".py", "").capitalize()
            script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)

            try:
                cmd = ["python", script_path, target_user]
                process = subprocess.Popen(cmd, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.PIPE, text=True, encoding="utf-8", bufsize=1)
                stdout_output, stderr_output = process.communicate()

                if stdout_output.strip():
                    print(f"✅ {system_name}: {stdout_output.strip()}")
                    access_list.append(system_name)

                if stderr_output.strip():
                    print(f"⚠️ {system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")
                    logging.error(f"{system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")

            except Exception as e:
                print(f"❌ {system_name}: Error checking access - {e}")
                logging.error(f"Error checking access for {system_name}: {e}")

    return access_list

# ✅ Remove access from a system
def remove_access(target_user, system_name, mock_mode):
    """Removes access from the selected system."""
    script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, f"remove_{system_name.lower()}.py")

    if os.path.exists(script_path):
        cmd = ["python", script_path, target_user]
        if mock_mode:
            cmd.append("--mock")

        subprocess.run(cmd, text=True, encoding="utf-8")
        print(f"✅ Removed access to {system_name} for {target_user}")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Remove script for {system_name} not found.")

# ✅ Grant access to a system
def grant_access(target_user, system_name, mock_mode):
    """Grants access to the selected system."""
    script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, f"grant_{system_name.lower()}.py")

    if os.path.exists(script_path):
        cmd = ["python", script_path, target_user]
        if mock_mode:
            cmd.append("--mock")

        subprocess.run(cmd, text=True, encoding="utf-8")
        print(f"✅ Granted access to {system_name} for {target_user}")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Grant script for {system_name} not found.")

# ✅ Main interactive workflow
def interactive_access_management():
    """Runs the interactive access management process."""

    # ✅ Simulate LDAP Credentials Instead of Fetching from Key Vault
    ldap_user = "mock_user@company.com"
    ldap_pass = "mock_password"

    # ✅ Retrieve LDAP credentials securely
    #ldap_user, ldap_pass = get_ldap_credentials()

    # ✅ Authenticate LDAP before proceeding
    if not authenticate_ldap(ldap_user, ldap_pass):
        print("❌ LDAP Authentication Failed. Access Denied.")
        sys.exit(1)

    # ✅ Get the target LDAP username
    target_user = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the LDAP username of the target user: ")

    # ✅ Check access first
    access_list = check_user_access(target_user)

    if access_list:
        print("\n🔹 The user currently has access to these systems:")
        for i, system in enumerate(access_list, start=1):
            print(f"  {i}. {system}")

        # ✅ Ask if access should be removed
        remove_choice = input("\nWould you like to remove access from any of these systems? (yes/no): ").strip().lower()
        if remove_choice == "yes":
            system_to_remove = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the system name to remove access from: ")
            if system_to_remove in access_list:
                remove_access(target_user, system_to_remove)
            else:
                print("❌ Invalid selection. System not found in the access list.")

    # ✅ Ask if access should be granted
    grant_choice = input("\nWould you like to grant access to a new system? (yes/no): ").strip().lower()
    if grant_choice == "yes":
        system_to_grant = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the system name to grant access to: ")
        grant_access(target_user, system_to_grant)

    print("\n🔹 Access management completed.")

# ✅ CLI Argument Parsing
if __name__ == "__main__":
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Manage SOC user access with LDAP authentication.")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode (for testing)")

    args = parser.parse_args()

    interactive_access_management(args.mock)

import requests
import getpass
import logging

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# Grafana API Configuration
GRAFANA_URL = "https://grafana.marchex.com"
GRAFANA_API_KEY = "your-api-key-here"  # Use an API key instead of login credentials

def authenticate_grafana(session, operatorUN, operatorPass, mock_mode):
    """ Authenticate with Grafana API (skipped in mock mode). """
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info("[MOCK] Skipping Grafana authentication.")
        return True

    login_url = f"{GRAFANA_URL}/login"
    credentials = {"user": operatorUN, "password": operatorPass}

    try:
        response = session.post(login_url, json=credentials)
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info("Successfully authenticated to Grafana.")
        return True
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to authenticate with Grafana: {e}")
        return False

def get_grafana_users(session, mock_mode):
    """ Fetch list of all Grafana users (mocked when MOCK_MODE=True). """
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info("[MOCK] Simulating Grafana user list retrieval.")
        return [{"login": "mockuser1"}, {"login": "mockadmin"}, {"login": "mockdev"}]  # Simulated users

    users_url = f"{GRAFANA_URL}/api/org/users"

    try:
        response = session.get(users_url, headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {GRAFANA_API_KEY}"})
        response.raise_for_status()
        return response.json()
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to retrieve Grafana users: {e}")
        return None

def main(user, creds):
    """ Check if a user has Grafana access. """
    mock_mode = creds["MOCK_MODE"]  # Read Mock Mode from creds
    operatorUN = creds["operatorUN"]
    operatorPass = creds["operatorPass"]

    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Checking Grafana access for {user}.")
        return (user, user, creds) if user in {"mockuser1", "mockadmin", "mockdev"} else (None, user, creds)

    with requests.Session() as session:
        if not authenticate_grafana(session, operatorUN, operatorPass, mock_mode):
            return None, user, creds

        grafana_users = get_grafana_users(session, mock_mode)

        if grafana_users is None:
            return None, user, creds

        # Check if the user exists in Grafana
        matching_users = [u for u in grafana_users if u["login"] == user]

        return (user, user, creds) if matching_users else (None, user, creds)

def foundAccess(result):
    """ Check if the user has Grafana access and remove if required. """
    if result[0]:
        user = result[1]
        accessChoice = result[2]["accessChoice"]
        mock_mode = result[2]["MOCK_MODE"]

        if accessChoice == "check":
            logging.info(f"{user} has Grafana access.")
        elif accessChoice == "remove":
            logging.info(f"{user} has Grafana access. Attempting removal...")
            deleteAccess(user, mock_mode)

def deleteAccess(user, mock_mode):
    """ Remove a user from Grafana. """
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would remove {user} from Grafana.")
        return  # Skip actual deletion in mock mode

    delete_url = f"{GRAFANA_URL}/api/admin/users/{user}"

    try:
        response = requests.delete(delete_url, headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {GRAFANA_API_KEY}"})
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info(f"Grafana access removed for {user}.")
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to remove Grafana access for {user}: {e}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    logging.info("Checking Grafana access...")

    operatorUN = input("Enter your LDAP username: ").strip()
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ").strip()
    users = input("Enter username(s) to check (comma-separated): ").strip().split(",")
    accessChoice = input("Would you like to check or remove access? (Check/Remove): ").strip().lower()

    while accessChoice not in ("remove", "check"):
        accessChoice = input("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check': ").strip().lower()

    creds = {
        "operatorUN": operatorUN,
        "operatorPass": operatorPass,
        "accessChoice": accessChoice,
        "MOCK_MODE": True  # This would be overridden when called from separations.py
    }

    for user in users:
        result = main(user.strip(), creds)
        foundAccess(result)





ok next lets look at the grafana.py script again this was previously only for check and remove of grafana access 4-5 years ago and i am being tasked with updating it, iv already updated it from python2 to python3, it now needs to be further modified and updated to not only check and remove access but also grant access per the SOC SOP.





SOC SOP uiAccessGrafana
SOC SOP uiAccessAWS | SOC SOP uiAccessGrafana
Jump to navigationJump to search
Description
This SOP is for adding and removing access for grafana.



Adding AccessRemoving Access

I believe that this instance below is the grafana that is associated with Kubernetes and infra owns that, so we may need them to grant access to this:

http://grafana1.us-east1.marchex.net/

1. Login to grafana as admin and select "add or invite users"

[Grafana users]

2. paste in the users email address into the tool and select the correct level of access. Then click invite users.

Removing Access

1. Login to grafana as admin, do a find for their user name, then click the red X.

[Grafana users]
import requests
import logging

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# JIRA API Configuration
JIRA_URL = "https://jira.marchex.com/rest/api/latest/user"
JIRA_API_TOKEN = "your_api_token_here"  # Use API Token instead of passwords
JIRA_USERNAME = "your_email@marchex.com"

def get_jira_headers():
    """Return the authentication headers for JIRA API."""
    return {
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {JIRA_API_TOKEN}",
        "Content-Type": "application/json"
    }

def check_jira_access(user, mock_mode):
    """Check if a user has access to JIRA (mocked if MOCK_MODE=True)."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating JIRA access check for {user}.")
        return f"{user} (Mock Display Name)" if user in ["mockuser", "testuser", "jiraadmin"] else None

    try:
        response = requests.get(
            f"{JIRA_URL}?username={user}",
            headers=get_jira_headers()
        )
        response.raise_for_status()
        data = response.json()

        if data.get("active", False):
            return f"{data['name']} ({data['displayName']})"
        else:
            return None

    except requests.exceptions.HTTPError as e:
        if response.status_code == 404:
            logging.warning(f"User {user} does not exist in JIRA.")
        else:
            logging.error(f"JIRA API request failed: {e}")
        return None
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Unexpected error while checking JIRA access: {e}")
        return None

def remove_jira_access(user, mock_mode):
    """Attempt to deactivate the user in JIRA (mocked when MOCK_MODE=True)."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would remove JIRA access for {user}.")
        return

    delete_url = f"https://jira.marchex.com/rest/api/latest/user?username={user}"

    try:
        response = requests.delete(delete_url, headers=get_jira_headers())

        if response.status_code == 204:
            logging.info(f"Successfully removed {user} from JIRA.")
        elif response.status_code == 403:
            logging.warning(f"Insufficient permissions to remove {user} from JIRA.")
        else:
            logging.error(f"Failed to remove {user} from JIRA: {response.text}")

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error during JIRA user removal: {e}")

def main(user, creds):
    """Check or remove JIRA access for a given user."""
    mock_mode = creds["MOCK_MODE"]  # Read Mock Mode from creds

    result = check_jira_access(user, mock_mode)

    if result:
        logging.info(f"{user} has JIRA access.")
        if creds["accessChoice"] == "remove":
            remove_jira_access(user, mock_mode)
    else:
        logging.info(f"{user} does not have JIRA access.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    logging.info("Checking JIRA access...")

    users = input("Enter username(s) to check (comma-separated): ").strip().split(",")
    accessChoice = input("Would you like to check or remove access? (Check/Remove): ").strip().lower()

    while accessChoice not in ("remove", "check"):
        accessChoice = input("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check': ").strip().lower()

    creds = {
        "accessChoice": accessChoice,
        "MOCK_MODE": True  # This would be overridden when called from separations.py
    }

    for user in users:
        main(user.strip(), creds)

SOC SOP uiAccessJIRA
SOC SOP uiAccessAWS | SOC SOP uiAccessGrafana | SOC SOP uiAccessJIRA
Jump to navigationJump to search
Description
This SOP is for adding and removing access to be able to use JIRA.

Adding AccessRemoving Access

When an account needs to be added by request/ticket use the following steps.




NOTE:
If the user is a contractor remove the "-c" from their alias.

1. Log onto [JIRA].

Log in method: Individual LDAP account


2. Click the Cog (Administration) > User Management

You will be prompted to log in again.


3. Search to check if the user already exists

Username/full name FILTER


4. If the user does not exist, click "Create User"

5. In the tool, select Delegated LDAP Authentication.

6. Fill out the following information and create the user:

Username (note: this must match the user's Marchex alias - get it from [Directory manager])
Full name
Email (Can be an @marchex.com or a non-marchex.com alias)
Check send notification box

7. Add the created user to necessary groups.

All users should be added to "jira-users" regardless of the request (you can't log in without this).
Add the user to any additional groups requested (if mirroring a user, add to all of that user's groups)
Check if they are an engineering user (they will be under the VP of engineering's org in the GAL). If they are, add them to "jira-ChangeControl" and "jira-developers" as well

Removing Access

When an account needs to be removed either from a separation or SOX audit or team change use the following steps.

1. Log onto [JIRA].

Log in method: Individual LDAP account

2. Click on the gear icon in the top right, and click on "user management"

You will need to re-verify your password

3. Search for the user in any of the available fields.

4. Click EDIT, and then de-select the "ACTIVE" checkbox and save.

5. If the UI states that the account cannot be deleted due to open tickets,
follow the next set of instructions:

Select the 'Quick Search' bar at the top right of the page and hit ENTER
Click 'ADVANCED' 
Type the following into the search bar: 
assignee = <USERID> AND status != Closed AND status != Done AND status != RESOLVED AND status != RESOLVED ORDER BY priority ASC
Reassign the tickets to the user's manager
Go back and delete the user as stated in step 3.

6. If the UI states that the account cannot be deleted because they are a component lead or project lead, follow the next set of instructions:

Assign the user's manager as new lead by following these steps:
Take note of which projects they are the lead for
Go to projects pulldown -> view all projects
Search for the project and click on it
Click project settings on the left
Click view project roles
Click edit defaults
Change the lead and click update
Now send an email to the user's manager informing them they've been assigned as lead. Ask that they pick a new lead at their convenience. 
Once the role has be re-assigned, go back and delete the user as stated in step 3.


For detailed information on how to deactivate a Jira account, see this page
import logging
import os
import cx_Oracle
import secret

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# Oracle DB Instances to check
DB_INSTANCES = ["OPNEXT"]

# Database Credentials
DB_USER = secret.get_secret("_ORACLE_USER")
DB_PASS = secret.get_secret("_ORACLE_PASS")
DB_DSN = secret.get_secret("_ORACLE_DSN")  # Example: "hostname:port/service_name"

# Check if Oracle Client is installed
try:
    cx_Oracle.init_oracle_client(lib_dir="/path/to/oracle_client")
except Exception as e:
    logging.error(f"Could not initialize Oracle client: {e}")
    exit(1)

def check_nimui_access(username, mock_mode):
    """Check if the user has access to NimUI (Oracle DB) (mocked when MOCK_MODE=True)."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating NimUI access check for {username}.")
        return [(1, username, f"{username}@marchex.com", "Active")] if username in ["mockuser", "testuser"] else None

    try:
        connection = cx_Oracle.connect(DB_USER, DB_PASS, DB_DSN)
        cursor = connection.cursor()

        query = """
        SELECT ID, USERNAME, EMAIL, STATUS
        FROM COMMON.USERS
        WHERE USERNAME = :username
        """

        cursor.execute(query, {"username": username})
        result = cursor.fetchall()

        cursor.close()
        connection.close()

        return result

    except cx_Oracle.DatabaseError as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to query NimUI for {username}: {e}")
        return None

def foundAccess(result, username, accessChoice, mock_mode):
    """Report user access status (mocked when MOCK_MODE=True)."""
    if result:
        if accessChoice == "check":
            logging.info(f"✅ {username} has NimUI access.")
        elif accessChoice == "remove":
            logging.warning(f"⚠️ {username} has NimUI access, but automatic removal is NOT available. Please remove manually.")
    else:
        logging.info(f"❌ {username} does NOT have NimUI access.")

def main(user, creds):
    """Check or remove NimUI access for a given user."""
    mock_mode = creds["MOCK_MODE"]  # Read Mock Mode from creds

    result = check_nimui_access(user, mock_mode)
    foundAccess(result, user, creds["accessChoice"], mock_mode)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    logging.info("Checking NimUI access...")

    username = input("Enter LDAP username to check/remove: ").strip()
    accessChoice = input("Would you like to check or remove access? (Check/Remove): ").strip().lower()

    while accessChoice not in ("check", "remove"):
        accessChoice = input("Invalid input. Please enter 'Check' or 'Remove': ").strip().lower()

    creds = {
        "accessChoice": accessChoice,
        "MOCK_MODE": True  # This would be overridden when called from separations.py
    }

    main(username, creds)

This SOP is for adding and removing access for the NimUI.

INSERT INTO COMMON.USERS (EMAIL,NAME,STATUS,USERNAME,USER_TYPE,PASSWORD) VALUES ('<EMAIL_ADDRESS>','<FIRST_NAME LAST_NAME>','A','<USERNAME>','internal','pending first login');
commit;
